[ ] 89470      r.eqSeen = 0;
[ ] 89471      rc = sqlite3BtreeMovetoUnpacked(pC->uc.pCursor, &r, 0, 0, &res);
[ ] 89472      if( rc!=SQLITE_OK ){
[ ] 89473        goto abort_due_to_error;
[ ] 89474      }
[ ] 89475      if( eqOnly && r.eqSeen==0 ){
[ ] 89476        assert( res!=0 );
[ ] 89477        goto seek_not_found;
[ ] 89478      }
[ ] 89479    }
[ ] 89480  #ifdef SQLITE_TEST
[ ] 89481    sqlite3_search_count++;
[ ] 89482  #endif
[ ] 89483    if( oc>=OP_SeekGE ){  assert( oc==OP_SeekGE || oc==OP_SeekGT );
[ ] 89484      if( res<0 || (res==0 && oc==OP_SeekGT) ){
[ ] 89485        res = 0;
[ ] 89486        rc = sqlite3BtreeNext(pC->uc.pCursor, 0);
[ ] 89487        if( rc!=SQLITE_OK ){
[ ] 89488          if( rc==SQLITE_DONE ){
[ ] 89489            rc = SQLITE_OK;
[ ] 89490            res = 1;
[ ] 89491          }else{
[ ] 89492            goto abort_due_to_error;
[ ] 89493          }
[ ] 89494        }
[ ] 89495      }else{
[ ] 89496        res = 0;
[ ] 89497      }
[ ] 89498    }else{
[ ] 89499      assert( oc==OP_SeekLT || oc==OP_SeekLE );
[ ] 89500      if( res>0 || (res==0 && oc==OP_SeekLT) ){
[ ] 89501        res = 0;
[ ] 89502        rc = sqlite3BtreePrevious(pC->uc.pCursor, 0);
[ ] 89503        if( rc!=SQLITE_OK ){
[ ] 89504          if( rc==SQLITE_DONE ){
[ ] 89505            rc = SQLITE_OK;
[ ] 89506            res = 1;
[ ] 89507          }else{
[ ] 89508            goto abort_due_to_error;
[ ] 89509          }
[ ] 89510        }
[ ] 89511      }else{
[ ] 89512        /* res might be negative because the table is empty.  Check to
[ ] 89513        ** see if this is the case.
[ ] 89514        */
[ ] 89515        res = sqlite3BtreeEof(pC->uc.pCursor);
[ ] 89516      }
[ ] 89517    }
[ ] 89518  seek_not_found:
[ ] 89519    assert( pOp->p2>0 );
[ ] 89520    VdbeBranchTaken(res!=0,2);
[ ] 89521    if( res ){
[ ] 89522      goto jump_to_p2;
[ ] 89523    }else if( eqOnly ){
[ ] 89524      assert( pOp[1].opcode==OP_IdxLT || pOp[1].opcode==OP_IdxGT );
[ ] 89525      pOp++; /* Skip the OP_IdxLt or OP_IdxGT that follows */
[ ] 89526    }
[ ] 89527    break;
[ ] 89528  }
[ ] 89529
[ ] 89530  /* Opcode: SeekHit P1 P2 * * *
[ ] 89531  ** Synopsis: seekHit=P2
[ ] 89532  **
[ ] 89533  ** Set the seekHit flag on cursor P1 to the value in P2.
[ ] 89534  * The seekHit flag is used by the IfNoHope opcode.
[ ] 89535  **
[ ] 89536  ** P1 must be a valid b-tree cursor.  P2 must be a boolean value,
[ ] 89537  ** either 0 or 1.
[ ] 89538  */
[ ] 89539  case OP_SeekHit: {
[ ] 89540    VdbeCursor *pC;
[ ] 89541    assert( pOp->p1>=0 && pOp->p1<p->nCursor );
[ ] 89542    pC = p->apCsr[pOp->p1];
[ ] 89543    assert( pC!=0 );
[ ] 89544    assert( pOp->p2==0 || pOp->p2==1 );
[ ] 89545    pC->seekHit = pOp->p2 & 1;
[ ] 89546    break;
[ ] 89547  }
[ ] 89548
[ ] 89549  /* Opcode: IfNotOpen P1 P2 * * *
[ ] 89550  ** Synopsis: if( !csr[P1] ) goto P2
[ ] 89551  **
[ ] 89552  ** If cursor P1 is not open, jump to instruction P2. Otherwise, fall through.
[ ] 89553  */
[ ] 89554  case OP_IfNotOpen: {        /* jump */
[ ] 89555    assert( pOp->p1>=0 && pOp->p1<p->nCursor );
[ ] 89556    VdbeBranchTaken(p->apCsr[pOp->p1]==0, 2);
[ ] 89557    if( !p->apCsr[pOp->p1] ){
[ ] 89558      goto jump_to_p2_and_check_for_interrupt;
[ ] 89559    }
[ ] 89560    break;
[ ] 89561  }
[ ] 89562
[ ] 89563  /* Opcode: Found P1 P2 P3 P4 *
[ ] 89564  ** Synopsis: key=r[P3@P4]
[ ] 89565  **
[ ] 89566  ** If P4==0 then register P3 holds a blob constructed by MakeRecord.  If
[ ] 89567  ** P4>0 then register P3 is the first of P4 registers that form an unpacked
[ ] 89568  ** record.
[ ] 89569  **
[ ] 89570  ** Cursor P1 is on an index btree.  If the record identified by P3 and P4
[ ] 89571  ** is a prefix of any entry in P1 then a jump is made to P2 and
[ ] 89572  ** P1 is left pointing at the matching entry.
[ ] 89573  **
[ ] 89574  ** This operation leaves the cursor in a state where it can be
[ ] 89575  ** advanced in the forward direction.  The Next instruction will work,
[ ] 89576  ** but not the Prev instruction.
[ ] 89577  **
[ ] 89578  ** See also: NotFound, NoConflict, NotExists. SeekGe
[ ] 89579  */
[ ] 89580  /* Opcode: NotFound P1 P2 P3 P4 *
[ ] 89581  ** Synopsis: key=r[P3@P4]
[ ] 89582  **
[ ] 89583  ** If P4==0 then register P3 holds a blob constructed by MakeRecord.  If
[ ] 89584  ** P4>0 then register P3 is the first of P4 registers that form an unpacked
[ ] 89585  ** record.
[ ] 89586  **
[ ] 89587  ** Cursor P1 is on an index btree.  If the record identified by P3 and P4
[ ] 89588  ** is not the prefix of any entry in P1 then a jump is made to P2.  If P1
[ ] 89589  ** does contain an entry whose prefix matches the P3/P4 record then control
[ ] 89590  ** falls through to the next instruction and P1 is left pointing at the
[ ] 89591  ** matching entry.
[ ] 89592  **
[ ] 89593  ** This operation leaves the cursor in a state where it cannot be
[ ] 89594  ** advanced in either direction.  In other words, the Next and Prev
[ ] 89595  ** opcodes do not work after this operation.
[ ] 89596  **
[ ] 89597  ** See also: Found, NotExists, NoConflict, IfNoHope
[ ] 89598  */
[ ] 89599  /* Opcode: IfNoHope P1 P2 P3 P4 *
[ ] 89600  ** Synopsis: key=r[P3@P4]
[ ] 89601  **
[ ] 89602  ** Register P3 is the first of P4 registers that form an unpacked
[ ] 89603  ** record.
[ ] 89604  **
[ ] 89605  ** Cursor P1 is on an index btree.  If the seekHit flag is set on P1, then
[ ] 89606  ** this opcode is a no-op.  But if the seekHit flag of P1 is clear, then
[ ] 89607  ** check to see if there is any entry in P1 that matches the
[ ] 89608  ** prefix identified by P3 and P4.  If no entry matches the prefix,
[ ] 89609  ** jump to P2.  Otherwise fall through.
[ ] 89610  **
[ ] 89611  ** This opcode behaves like OP_NotFound if the seekHit
[ ] 89612  ** flag is clear and it behaves like OP_Noop if the seekHit flag is set.
[ ] 89613  **
[ ] 89614  ** This opcode is used in IN clause processing for a multi-column key.
[ ] 89615  ** If an IN clause is attached to an element of the key other than the
[ ] 89616  ** left-most element, and if there are no matches on the most recent
[ ] 89617  ** seek over the whole key, then it might be that one of the key element
[ ] 89618  ** to the left is prohibiting a match, and hence there is "no hope" of
[ ] 89619  ** any match regardless of how many IN clause elements are checked.
[ ] 89620  ** In such a case, we abandon the IN clause search early, using this
[ ] 89621  ** opcode.  The opcode name comes from the fact that the
[ ] 89622  ** jump is taken if there is "no hope" of achieving a match.
[ ] 89623  **
[ ] 89624  ** See also: NotFound, SeekHit
[ ] 89625  */
[ ] 89626  /* Opcode: NoConflict P1 P2 P3 P4 *
[ ] 89627  ** Synopsis: key=r[P3@P4]
[ ] 89628  **
[ ] 89629  ** If P4==0 then register P3 holds a blob constructed by MakeRecord.  If
[ ] 89630  ** P4>0 then register P3 is the first of P4 registers that form an unpacked
[ ] 89631  ** record.
[ ] 89632  **
[ ] 89633  ** Cursor P1 is on an index btree.  If the record identified by P3 and P4
[ ] 89634  ** contains any NULL value, jump immediately to P2.  If all terms of the
[ ] 89635  ** record are not-NULL then a check is done to determine if any row in the
[ ] 89636  ** P1 index btree has a matching key prefix.  If there are no matches, jump
[ ] 89637  ** immediately to P2.  If there is a match, fall through and leave the P1
[ ] 89638  ** cursor pointing to the matching row.
[ ] 89639  **
[ ] 89640  ** This opcode is similar to OP_NotFound with the exceptions that the
[ ] 89641  ** branch is always taken if any part of the search key input is NULL.
[ ] 89642  **
[ ] 89643  ** This operation leaves the cursor in a state where it cannot be
[ ] 89644  ** advanced in either direction.  In other words, the Next and Prev
[ ] 89645  ** opcodes do not work after this operation.
[ ] 89646  **
[ ] 89647  ** See also: NotFound, Found, NotExists
[ ] 89648  */
[ ] 89649  case OP_IfNoHope: {     /* jump, in3 */
[ ] 89650    VdbeCursor *pC;
[ ] 89651    assert( pOp->p1>=0 && pOp->p1<p->nCursor );
[ ] 89652    pC = p->apCsr[pOp->p1];
[ ] 89653    assert( pC!=0 );
[ ] 89654    if( pC->seekHit ) break;
[ ] 89655    /* Fall through into OP_NotFound */
[ ] 89656  }
[ ] 89657  case OP_NoConflict:     /* jump, in3 */
[ ] 89658  case OP_NotFound:       /* jump, in3 */
[ ] 89659  case OP_Found: {        /* jump, in3 */
[ ] 89660    int alreadyExists;
[ ] 89661    int takeJump;
[ ] 89662    int ii;
[ ] 89663    VdbeCursor *pC;
[ ] 89664    int res;
[ ] 89665    UnpackedRecord *pFree;
[ ] 89666    UnpackedRecord *pIdxKey;
[ ] 89667    UnpackedRecord r;
[ ] 89668
[ ] 89669  #ifdef SQLITE_TEST
[ ] 89670    if( pOp->opcode!=OP_NoConflict ) sqlite3_found_count++;
[ ] 89671  #endif
[ ] 89672
[ ] 89673    assert( pOp->p1>=0 && pOp->p1<p->nCursor );
[ ] 89674    assert( pOp->p4type==P4_INT32 );
[ ] 89675    pC = p->apCsr[pOp->p1];
[ ] 89676    assert( pC!=0 );
[ ] 89677  #ifdef SQLITE_DEBUG
[ ] 89678    pC->seekOp = pOp->opcode;
[ ] 89679  #endif
[ ] 89680    pIn3 = &aMem[pOp->p3];
[ ] 89681    assert( pC->eCurType==CURTYPE_BTREE );
[ ] 89682    assert( pC->uc.pCursor!=0 );
[ ] 89683    assert( pC->isTable==0 );
[ ] 89684    if( pOp->p4.i>0 ){
[ ] 89685      r.pKeyInfo = pC->pKeyInfo;
[ ] 89686      r.nField = (u16)pOp->p4.i;
[ ] 89687      r.aMem = pIn3;
[ ] 89688  #ifdef SQLITE_DEBUG
[ ] 89689      for(ii=0; ii<r.nField; ii++){
[ ] 89690        assert( memIsValid(&r.aMem[ii]) );
[ ] 89691        assert( (r.aMem[ii].flags & MEM_Zero)==0 || r.aMem[ii].n==0 );
[ ] 89692        if( ii ) REGISTER_TRACE(pOp->p3+ii, &r.aMem[ii]);
[ ] 89693      }
[ ] 89694  #endif
[ ] 89695      pIdxKey = &r;
[ ] 89696      pFree = 0;
[ ] 89697    }else{
[ ] 89698      assert( pIn3->flags & MEM_Blob );
[ ] 89699      rc = ExpandBlob(pIn3);
[ ] 89700      assert( rc==SQLITE_OK || rc==SQLITE_NOMEM );
[ ] 89701      if( rc ) goto no_mem;
[ ] 89702      pFree = pIdxKey = sqlite3VdbeAllocUnpackedRecord(pC->pKeyInfo);
[ ] 89703      if( pIdxKey==0 ) goto no_mem;
[ ] 89704      sqlite3VdbeRecordUnpack(pC->pKeyInfo, pIn3->n, pIn3->z, pIdxKey);
[ ] 89705    }
[ ] 89706    pIdxKey->default_rc = 0;
[ ] 89707    takeJump = 0;
[ ] 89708    if( pOp->opcode==OP_NoConflict ){
[ ] 89709      /* For the OP_NoConflict opcode, take the jump if any of the
[ ] 89710      ** input fields are NULL, since any key with a NULL will not
[ ] 89711      ** conflict */
[ ] 89712      for(ii=0; ii<pIdxKey->nField; ii++){
[ ] 89713        if( pIdxKey->aMem[ii].flags & MEM_Null ){
[ ] 89714          takeJump = 1;
[ ] 89715          break;
[ ] 89716        }
[ ] 89717      }
[ ] 89718    }
[ ] 89719    rc = sqlite3BtreeMovetoUnpacked(pC->uc.pCursor, pIdxKey, 0, 0, &res);
[ ] 89720    if( pFree ) sqlite3DbFreeNN(db, pFree);
[ ] 89721    if( rc!=SQLITE_OK ){
[ ] 89722      goto abort_due_to_error;
[ ] 89723    }
[ ] 89724    pC->seekResult = res;
[ ] 89725    alreadyExists = (res==0);
[ ] 89726    pC->nullRow = 1-alreadyExists;
[ ] 89727    pC->deferredMoveto = 0;
[ ] 89728    pC->cacheStatus = CACHE_STALE;
[ ] 89729    if( pOp->opcode==OP_Found ){
[ ] 89730      VdbeBranchTaken(alreadyExists!=0,2);
[ ] 89731      if( alreadyExists ) goto jump_to_p2;
[ ] 89732    }else{
[ ] 89733      VdbeBranchTaken(takeJump||alreadyExists==0,2);
[ ] 89734      if( takeJump || !alreadyExists ) goto jump_to_p2;
[ ] 89735    }
[ ] 89736    break;
[ ] 89737  }
[ ] 89738
[ ] 89739  /* Opcode: SeekRowid P1 P2 P3 * *
[ ] 89740  ** Synopsis: intkey=r[P3]
[ ] 89741  **
[ ] 89742  ** P1 is the index of a cursor open on an SQL table btree (with integer
[ ] 89743  ** keys).  If register P3 does not contain an integer or if P1 does not
[ ] 89744  ** contain a record with rowid P3 then jump immediately to P2.
[ ] 89745  ** Or, if P2 is 0, raise an SQLITE_CORRUPT error. If P1 does contain
[ ] 89746  ** a record with rowid P3 then
[ ] 89747  ** leave the cursor pointing at that record and fall through to the next
[ ] 89748  ** instruction.
[ ] 89749  **
[ ] 89750  ** The OP_NotExists opcode performs the same operation, but with OP_NotExists
[ ] 89751  ** the P3 register must be guaranteed to contain an integer value.  With this
[ ] 89752  ** opcode, register P3 might not contain an integer.
[ ] 89753  **
[ ] 89754  ** The OP_NotFound opcode performs the same operation on index btrees
[ ] 89755  ** (with arbitrary multi-value keys).
[ ] 89756  **
[ ] 89757  ** This opcode leaves the cursor in a state where it cannot be advanced
[ ] 89758  ** in either direction.  In other words, the Next and Prev opcodes will
[ ] 89759  ** not work following this opcode.
[ ] 89760  **
[ ] 89761  ** See also: Found, NotFound, NoConflict, SeekRowid
[ ] 89762  */
[ ] 89763  /* Opcode: NotExists P1 P2 P3 * *
[ ] 89764  ** Synopsis: intkey=r[P3]
[ ] 89765  **
[ ] 89766  ** P1 is the index of a cursor open on an SQL table btree (with integer
[ ] 89767  ** keys).  P3 is an integer rowid.  If P1 does not contain a record with
[ ] 89768  ** rowid P3 then jump immediately to P2.  Or, if P2 is 0, raise an
[ ] 89769  ** SQLITE_CORRUPT error. If P1 does contain a record with rowid P3 then
[ ] 89770  ** leave the cursor pointing at that record and fall through to the next
[ ] 89771  ** instruction.
[ ] 89772  **
[ ] 89773  ** The OP_SeekRowid opcode performs the same operation but also allows the
[ ] 89774  ** P3 register to contain a non-integer value, in which case the jump is
[ ] 89775  ** always taken.  This opcode requires that P3 always contain an integer.
[ ] 89776  **
[ ] 89777  ** The OP_NotFound opcode performs the same operation on index btrees
[ ] 89778  ** (with arbitrary multi-value keys).
[ ] 89779  **
[ ] 89780  ** This opcode leaves the cursor in a state where it cannot be advanced
[ ] 89781  ** in either direction.  In other words, the Next and Prev opcodes will
[ ] 89782  ** not work following this opcode.
[ ] 89783  **
[ ] 89784  ** See also: Found, NotFound, NoConflict, SeekRowid
[ ] 89785  */
[ ] 89786  case OP_SeekRowid: {        /* jump, in3 */
[ ] 89787    VdbeCursor *pC;
[ ] 89788    BtCursor *pCrsr;
[ ] 89789    int res;
[ ] 89790    u64 iKey;
[ ] 89791
[ ] 89792    pIn3 = &aMem[pOp->p3];
[ ] 89793    testcase( pIn3->flags & MEM_Int );
[ ] 89794    testcase( pIn3->flags & MEM_IntReal );
[ ] 89795    testcase( pIn3->flags & MEM_Real );
[ ] 89796    testcase( (pIn3->flags & (MEM_Str|MEM_Int))==MEM_Str );
[ ] 89797    if( (pIn3->flags & (MEM_Int|MEM_IntReal))==0 ){
[ ] 89798      /* If pIn3->u.i does not contain an integer, compute iKey as the
[ ] 89799      ** integer value of pIn3.  Jump to P2 if pIn3 cannot be converted
[ ] 89800      ** into an integer without loss of information.  Take care to avoid
[ ] 89801      ** changing the datatype of pIn3, however, as it is used by other
[ ] 89802      ** parts of the prepared statement. */
[ ] 89803      Mem x = pIn3[0];
[ ] 89804      applyAffinity(&x, SQLITE_AFF_NUMERIC, encoding);
[ ] 89805      if( (x.flags & MEM_Int)==0 ) goto jump_to_p2;
[ ] 89806      iKey = x.u.i;
[ ] 89807      goto notExistsWithKey;
[ ] 89808    }
[ ] 89809    /* Fall through into OP_NotExists */
[ ] 89810  case OP_NotExists:          /* jump, in3 */
[ ] 89811    pIn3 = &aMem[pOp->p3];
[ ] 89812    assert( (pIn3->flags & MEM_Int)!=0 || pOp->opcode==OP_SeekRowid );
[ ] 89813    assert( pOp->p1>=0 && pOp->p1<p->nCursor );
[ ] 89814    iKey = pIn3->u.i;
[ ] 89815  notExistsWithKey:
[ ] 89816    pC = p->apCsr[pOp->p1];
[ ] 89817    assert( pC!=0 );
[ ] 89818  #ifdef SQLITE_DEBUG
[ ] 89819    if( pOp->opcode==OP_SeekRowid ) pC->seekOp = OP_SeekRowid;
[ ] 89820  #endif
[ ] 89821    assert( pC->isTable );
[ ] 89822    assert( pC->eCurType==CURTYPE_BTREE );
[ ] 89823    pCrsr = pC->uc.pCursor;
[ ] 89824    assert( pCrsr!=0 );
[ ] 89825    res = 0;
[ ] 89826    rc = sqlite3BtreeMovetoUnpacked(pCrsr, 0, iKey, 0, &res);
[ ] 89827    assert( rc==SQLITE_OK || res==0 );
[ ] 89828    pC->movetoTarget = iKey;  /* Used by OP_Delete */
[ ] 89829    pC->nullRow = 0;
[ ] 89830    pC->cacheStatus = CACHE_STALE;
[ ] 89831    pC->deferredMoveto = 0;
[ ] 89832    VdbeBranchTaken(res!=0,2);
[ ] 89833    pC->seekResult = res;
[ ] 89834    if( res!=0 ){
[ ] 89835      assert( rc==SQLITE_OK );
[ ] 89836      if( pOp->p2==0 ){
[ ] 89837        rc = SQLITE_CORRUPT_BKPT;
[ ] 89838      }else{
[ ] 89839        goto jump_to_p2;
[ ] 89840      }
[ ] 89841    }
[ ] 89842    if( rc ) goto abort_due_to_error;
[ ] 89843    break;
[ ] 89844  }
[ ] 89845
[ ] 89846  /* Opcode: Sequence P1 P2 * * *
[ ] 89847  ** Synopsis: r[P2]=cursor[P1].ctr++
[ ] 89848  **
[ ] 89849  ** Find the next available sequence number for cursor P1.
[ ] 89850  ** Write the sequence number into register P2.
[ ] 89851  ** The sequence number on the cursor is incremented after this
[ ] 89852  ** instruction.
[ ] 89853  */
[ ] 89854  case OP_Sequence: {           /* out2 */
[ ] 89855    assert( pOp->p1>=0 && pOp->p1<p->nCursor );
[ ] 89856    assert( p->apCsr[pOp->p1]!=0 );
[ ] 89857    assert( p->apCsr[pOp->p1]->eCurType!=CURTYPE_VTAB );
[ ] 89858    pOut = out2Prerelease(p, pOp);
[ ] 89859    pOut->u.i = p->apCsr[pOp->p1]->seqCount++;
[ ] 89860    break;
[ ] 89861  }
[ ] 89862
[ ] 89863
[ ] 89864  /* Opcode: NewRowid P1 P2 P3 * *
[ ] 89865  ** Synopsis: r[P2]=rowid
[ ] 89866  **
[ ] 89867  ** Get a new integer record number (a.k.a "rowid") used as the key to a table.
[ ] 89868  ** The record number is not previously used as a key in the database
[ ] 89869  ** table that cursor P1 points to.  The new record number is written
[ ] 89870  ** written to register P2.
[ ] 89871  **
[ ] 89872  ** If P3>0 then P3 is a register in the root frame of this VDBE that holds
[ ] 89873  ** the largest previously generated record number. No new record numbers are
[ ] 89874  ** allowed to be less than this value. When this value reaches its maximum,
[ ] 89875  ** an SQLITE_FULL error is generated. The P3 register is updated with the '
[ ] 89876  ** generated record number. This P3 mechanism is used to help implement the
[ ] 89877  ** AUTOINCREMENT feature.
[ ] 89878  */
[ ] 89879  case OP_NewRowid: {           /* out2 */
[ ] 89880    i64 v;                 /* The new rowid */
[ ] 89881    VdbeCursor *pC;        /* Cursor of table to get the new rowid */
[ ] 89882    int res;               /* Result of an sqlite3BtreeLast() */
[ ] 89883    int cnt;               /* Counter to limit the number of searches */
[ ] 89884    Mem *pMem;             /* Register holding largest rowid for AUTOINCREMENT */
[ ] 89885    VdbeFrame *pFrame;     /* Root frame of VDBE */
[ ] 89886
[ ] 89887    v = 0;
[ ] 89888    res = 0;
[ ] 89889    pOut = out2Prerelease(p, pOp);
[ ] 89890    assert( pOp->p1>=0 && pOp->p1<p->nCursor );
[ ] 89891    pC = p->apCsr[pOp->p1];
[ ] 89892    assert( pC!=0 );
[ ] 89893    assert( pC->isTable );
[ ] 89894    assert( pC->eCurType==CURTYPE_BTREE );
[ ] 89895    assert( pC->uc.pCursor!=0 );
[ ] 89896    {
[ ] 89897      /* The next rowid or record number (different terms for the same
[ ] 89898      ** thing) is obtained in a two-step algorithm.
[ ] 89899      **
[ ] 89900      ** First we attempt to find the largest existing rowid and add one
[ ] 89901      ** to that.  But if the largest existing rowid is already the maximum
[ ] 89902      ** positive integer, we have to fall through to the second
[ ] 89903      ** probabilistic algorithm
[ ] 89904      **
[ ] 89905      ** The second algorithm is to select a rowid at random and see if
[ ] 89906      ** it already exists in the table.  If it does not exist, we have
[ ] 89907      ** succeeded.  If the random rowid does exist, we select a new one
[ ] 89908      ** and try again, up to 100 times.
[ ] 89909      */
[ ] 89910      assert( pC->isTable );
[ ] 89911
[ ] 89912  #ifdef SQLITE_32BIT_ROWID
[ ] 89913  #   define MAX_ROWID 0x7fffffff
[ ] 89914  #else
[ ] 89915      /* Some compilers complain about constants of the form 0x7fffffffffffffff.
[ ] 89916      ** Others complain about 0x7ffffffffffffffffLL.  The following macro seems
[ ] 89917      ** to provide the constant while making all compilers happy.
[ ] 89918      */
[ ] 89919  #   define MAX_ROWID  (i64)( (((u64)0x7fffffff)<<32) | (u64)0xffffffff )
[ ] 89920  #endif
[ ] 89921
[ ] 89922      if( !pC->useRandomRowid ){
[ ] 89923        rc = sqlite3BtreeLast(pC->uc.pCursor, &res);
[ ] 89924        if( rc!=SQLITE_OK ){
[ ] 89925          goto abort_due_to_error;
[ ] 89926        }
[ ] 89927        if( res ){
[ ] 89928          v = 1;   /* IMP: R-61914-48074 */
[ ] 89929        }else{
[ ] 89930          assert( sqlite3BtreeCursorIsValid(pC->uc.pCursor) );
[ ] 89931          v = sqlite3BtreeIntegerKey(pC->uc.pCursor);
[ ] 89932          if( v>=MAX_ROWID ){
[ ] 89933            pC->useRandomRowid = 1;
[ ] 89934          }else{
[ ] 89935            v++;   /* IMP: R-29538-34987 */
[ ] 89936          }
[ ] 89937        }
[ ] 89938      }
[ ] 89939
[ ] 89940  #ifndef SQLITE_OMIT_AUTOINCREMENT
[ ] 89941      if( pOp->p3 ){
[ ] 89942        /* Assert that P3 is a valid memory cell. */
[ ] 89943        assert( pOp->p3>0 );
[ ] 89944        if( p->pFrame ){
[ ] 89945          for(pFrame=p->pFrame; pFrame->pParent; pFrame=pFrame->pParent);
[ ] 89946          /* Assert that P3 is a valid memory cell. */
[ ] 89947          assert( pOp->p3<=pFrame->nMem );
[ ] 89948          pMem = &pFrame->aMem[pOp->p3];
[ ] 89949        }else{
[ ] 89950          /* Assert that P3 is a valid memory cell. */
[ ] 89951          assert( pOp->p3<=(p->nMem+1 - p->nCursor) );
[ ] 89952          pMem = &aMem[pOp->p3];
[ ] 89953          memAboutToChange(p, pMem);
[ ] 89954        }
[ ] 89955        assert( memIsValid(pMem) );
[ ] 89956
[ ] 89957        REGISTER_TRACE(pOp->p3, pMem);
[ ] 89958        sqlite3VdbeMemIntegerify(pMem);
[ ] 89959        assert( (pMem->flags & MEM_Int)!=0 );  /* mem(P3) holds an integer */
[ ] 89960        if( pMem->u.i==MAX_ROWID || pC->useRandomRowid ){
[ ] 89961          rc = SQLITE_FULL;   /* IMP: R-17817-00630 */
[ ] 89962          goto abort_due_to_error;
[ ] 89963        }
[ ] 89964        if( v<pMem->u.i+1 ){
[ ] 89965          v = pMem->u.i + 1;
[ ] 89966        }
[ ] 89967        pMem->u.i = v;
[ ] 89968      }
[ ] 89969  #endif
[ ] 89970      if( pC->useRandomRowid ){
[ ] 89971        /* IMPLEMENTATION-OF: R-07677-41881 If the largest ROWID is equal to the
[ ] 89972        ** largest possible integer (9223372036854775807) then the database
[ ] 89973        ** engine starts picking positive candidate ROWIDs at random until
[ ] 89974        ** it finds one that is not previously used. */
[ ] 89975        assert( pOp->p3==0 );  /* We cannot be in random rowid mode if this is
[ ] 89976                               ** an AUTOINCREMENT table. */
[ ] 89977        cnt = 0;
[ ] 89978        do{
[ ] 89979          sqlite3_randomness(sizeof(v), &v);
[ ] 89980          v &= (MAX_ROWID>>1); v++;  /* Ensure that v is greater than zero */
[ ] 89981        }while(  ((rc = sqlite3BtreeMovetoUnpacked(pC->uc.pCursor, 0, (u64)v,
[ ] 89982                                                   0, &res))==SQLITE_OK)
[ ] 89983              && (res==0)
[ ] 89984              && (++cnt<100));
[ ] 89985        if( rc ) goto abort_due_to_error;
[ ] 89986        if( res==0 ){
[ ] 89987          rc = SQLITE_FULL;   /* IMP: R-38219-53002 */
[ ] 89988          goto abort_due_to_error;
[ ] 89989        }
[ ] 89990        assert( v>0 );  /* EV: R-40812-03570 */
[ ] 89991      }
[ ] 89992      pC->deferredMoveto = 0;
[ ] 89993      pC->cacheStatus = CACHE_STALE;
[ ] 89994    }
[ ] 89995    pOut->u.i = v;
[ ] 89996    break;
[ ] 89997  }
[ ] 89998
[ ] 89999  /* Opcode: Insert P1 P2 P3 P4 P5
[ ] 90000  ** Synopsis: intkey=r[P3] data=r[P2]
[ ] 90001  **
[ ] 90002  ** Write an entry into the table of cursor P1.  A new entry is
[ ] 90003  ** created if it doesn't already exist or the data for an existing
[ ] 90004  ** entry is overwritten.  The data is the value MEM_Blob stored in register
[ ] 90005  ** number P2. The key is stored in register P3. The key must
[ ] 90006  ** be a MEM_Int.
[ ] 90007  **
[ ] 90008  ** If the OPFLAG_NCHANGE flag of P5 is set, then the row change count is
[ ] 90009  ** incremented (otherwise not).  If the OPFLAG_LASTROWID flag of P5 is set,
[ ] 90010  ** then rowid is stored for subsequent return by the
[ ] 90011  ** sqlite3_last_insert_rowid() function (otherwise it is unmodified).
[ ] 90012  **
[ ] 90013  ** If the OPFLAG_USESEEKRESULT flag of P5 is set, the implementation might
[ ] 90014  ** run faster by avoiding an unnecessary seek on cursor P1.  However,
[ ] 90015  ** the OPFLAG_USESEEKRESULT flag must only be set if there have been no prior
[ ] 90016  ** seeks on the cursor or if the most recent seek used a key equal to P3.
[ ] 90017  **
[ ] 90018  ** If the OPFLAG_ISUPDATE flag is set, then this opcode is part of an
[ ] 90019  ** UPDATE operation.  Otherwise (if the flag is clear) then this opcode
[ ] 90020  ** is part of an INSERT operation.  The difference is only important to
[ ] 90021  ** the update hook.
[ ] 90022  **
[ ] 90023  ** Parameter P4 may point to a Table structure, or may be NULL. If it is
[ ] 90024  ** not NULL, then the update-hook (sqlite3.xUpdateCallback) is invoked
[ ] 90025  ** following a successful insert.
[ ] 90026  **
[ ] 90027  ** (WARNING/TODO: If P1 is a pseudo-cursor and P2 is dynamically
[ ] 90028  ** allocated, then ownership of P2 is transferred to the pseudo-cursor
[ ] 90029  ** and register P2 becomes ephemeral.  If the cursor is changed, the
[ ] 90030  ** value of register P2 will then change.  Make sure this does not
[ ] 90031  ** cause any problems.)
[ ] 90032  **
[ ] 90033  ** This instruction only works on tables.  The equivalent instruction
[ ] 90034  ** for indices is OP_IdxInsert.
[ ] 90035  */
[ ] 90036  case OP_Insert: {
[ ] 90037    Mem *pData;       /* MEM cell holding data for the record to be inserted */
[ ] 90038    Mem *pKey;        /* MEM cell holding key  for the record */
[ ] 90039    VdbeCursor *pC;   /* Cursor to table into which insert is written */
[ ] 90040    int seekResult;   /* Result of prior seek or 0 if no USESEEKRESULT flag */
[ ] 90041    const char *zDb;  /* database name - used by the update hook */
[ ] 90042    Table *pTab;      /* Table structure - used by update and pre-update hooks */
[ ] 90043    BtreePayload x;   /* Payload to be inserted */
[ ] 90044
[ ] 90045    pData = &aMem[pOp->p2];
[ ] 90046    assert( pOp->p1>=0 && pOp->p1<p->nCursor );
[ ] 90047    assert( memIsValid(pData) );
[ ] 90048    pC = p->apCsr[pOp->p1];
[ ] 90049    assert( pC!=0 );
[ ] 90050    assert( pC->eCurType==CURTYPE_BTREE );
[ ] 90051    assert( pC->deferredMoveto==0 );
[ ] 90052    assert( pC->uc.pCursor!=0 );
[ ] 90053    assert( (pOp->p5 & OPFLAG_ISNOOP) || pC->isTable );
[ ] 90054    assert( pOp->p4type==P4_TABLE || pOp->p4type>=P4_STATIC );
[ ] 90055    REGISTER_TRACE(pOp->p2, pData);
[ ] 90056    sqlite3VdbeIncrWriteCounter(p, pC);
[ ] 90057
[ ] 90058    pKey = &aMem[pOp->p3];
[ ] 90059    assert( pKey->flags & MEM_Int );
[ ] 90060    assert( memIsValid(pKey) );
[ ] 90061    REGISTER_TRACE(pOp->p3, pKey);
[ ] 90062    x.nKey = pKey->u.i;
[ ] 90063
[ ] 90064    if( pOp->p4type==P4_TABLE && HAS_UPDATE_HOOK(db) ){
[ ] 90065      assert( pC->iDb>=0 );
[ ] 90066      zDb = db->aDb[pC->iDb].zDbSName;
[ ] 90067      pTab = pOp->p4.pTab;
[ ] 90068      assert( (pOp->p5 & OPFLAG_ISNOOP) || HasRowid(pTab) );
[ ] 90069    }else{
[ ] 90070      pTab = 0;
[ ] 90071      zDb = 0;  /* Not needed.  Silence a compiler warning. */
[ ] 90072    }
[ ] 90073
[ ] 90074  #ifdef SQLITE_ENABLE_PREUPDATE_HOOK
[ ] 90075    /* Invoke the pre-update hook, if any */
[ ] 90076    if( pTab ){
[ ] 90077      if( db->xPreUpdateCallback && !(pOp->p5 & OPFLAG_ISUPDATE) ){
[ ] 90078        sqlite3VdbePreUpdateHook(p, pC, SQLITE_INSERT, zDb, pTab, x.nKey,pOp->p2);
[ ] 90079      }
[ ] 90080      if( db->xUpdateCallback==0 || pTab->aCol==0 ){
[ ] 90081        /* Prevent post-update hook from running in cases when it should not */
[ ] 90082        pTab = 0;
[ ] 90083      }
[ ] 90084    }
[ ] 90085    if( pOp->p5 & OPFLAG_ISNOOP ) break;
[ ] 90086  #endif
[ ] 90087
[ ] 90088    if( pOp->p5 & OPFLAG_NCHANGE ) p->nChange++;
[ ] 90089    if( pOp->p5 & OPFLAG_LASTROWID ) db->lastRowid = x.nKey;
[ ] 90090    assert( pData->flags & (MEM_Blob|MEM_Str) );
[ ] 90091    x.pData = pData->z;
[ ] 90092    x.nData = pData->n;
[ ] 90093    seekResult = ((pOp->p5 & OPFLAG_USESEEKRESULT) ? pC->seekResult : 0);
[ ] 90094    if( pData->flags & MEM_Zero ){
[ ] 90095      x.nZero = pData->u.nZero;
[ ] 90096    }else{
[ ] 90097      x.nZero = 0;
[ ] 90098    }
[ ] 90099    x.pKey = 0;
[ ] 90100    rc = sqlite3BtreeInsert(pC->uc.pCursor, &x,
[ ] 90101        (pOp->p5 & (OPFLAG_APPEND|OPFLAG_SAVEPOSITION)), seekResult
[ ] 90102    );
[ ] 90103    pC->deferredMoveto = 0;
[ ] 90104    pC->cacheStatus = CACHE_STALE;
[ ] 90105
[ ] 90106    /* Invoke the update-hook if required. */
[ ] 90107    if( rc ) goto abort_due_to_error;
[ ] 90108    if( pTab ){
[ ] 90109      assert( db->xUpdateCallback!=0 );
[ ] 90110      assert( pTab->aCol!=0 );
[ ] 90111      db->xUpdateCallback(db->pUpdateArg,
[ ] 90112             (pOp->p5 & OPFLAG_ISUPDATE) ? SQLITE_UPDATE : SQLITE_INSERT,
[ ] 90113             zDb, pTab->zName, x.nKey);
[ ] 90114    }
[ ] 90115    break;
[ ] 90116  }
[ ] 90117
[ ] 90118  /* Opcode: Delete P1 P2 P3 P4 P5
[ ] 90119  **
[ ] 90120  ** Delete the record at which the P1 cursor is currently pointing.
[ ] 90121  **
[ ] 90122  ** If the OPFLAG_SAVEPOSITION bit of the P5 parameter is set, then
[ ] 90123  ** the cursor will be left pointing at  either the next or the previous
[ ] 90124  ** record in the table. If it is left pointing at the next record, then
[ ] 90125  ** the next Next instruction will be a no-op. As a result, in this case
[ ] 90126  ** it is ok to delete a record from within a Next loop. If
[ ] 90127  ** OPFLAG_SAVEPOSITION bit of P5 is clear, then the cursor will be
[ ] 90128  ** left in an undefined state.
[ ] 90129  **
[ ] 90130  ** If the OPFLAG_AUXDELETE bit is set on P5, that indicates that this
[ ] 90131  ** delete one of several associated with deleting a table row and all its
[ ] 90132  ** associated index entries.  Exactly one of those deletes is the "primary"
[ ] 90133  ** delete.  The others are all on OPFLAG_FORDELETE cursors or else are
[ ] 90134  ** marked with the AUXDELETE flag.
[ ] 90135  **
[ ] 90136  ** If the OPFLAG_NCHANGE flag of P2 (NB: P2 not P5) is set, then the row
[ ] 90137  ** change count is incremented (otherwise not).
[ ] 90138  **
[ ] 90139  ** P1 must not be pseudo-table.  It has to be a real table with
[ ] 90140  ** multiple rows.
[ ] 90141  **
[ ] 90142  ** If P4 is not NULL then it points to a Table object. In this case either
[ ] 90143  ** the update or pre-update hook, or both, may be invoked. The P1 cursor must
[ ] 90144  ** have been positioned using OP_NotFound prior to invoking this opcode in
[ ] 90145  ** this case. Specifically, if one is configured, the pre-update hook is
[ ] 90146  ** invoked if P4 is not NULL. The update-hook is invoked if one is configured,
[ ] 90147  ** P4 is not NULL, and the OPFLAG_NCHANGE flag is set in P2.
[ ] 90148  **
[ ] 90149  ** If the OPFLAG_ISUPDATE flag is set in P2, then P3 contains the address
[ ] 90150  ** of the memory cell that contains the value that the rowid of the row will
[ ] 90151  ** be set to by the update.
[ ] 90152  */
[ ] 90153  case OP_Delete: {
[ ] 90154    VdbeCursor *pC;
[ ] 90155    const char *zDb;
[ ] 90156    Table *pTab;
[ ] 90157    int opflags;
[ ] 90158
[ ] 90159    opflags = pOp->p2;
[ ] 90160    assert( pOp->p1>=0 && pOp->p1<p->nCursor );
[ ] 90161    pC = p->apCsr[pOp->p1];
[ ] 90162    assert( pC!=0 );
[ ] 90163    assert( pC->eCurType==CURTYPE_BTREE );
[ ] 90164    assert( pC->uc.pCursor!=0 );
[ ] 90165    assert( pC->deferredMoveto==0 );
[ ] 90166    sqlite3VdbeIncrWriteCounter(p, pC);
[ ] 90167
[ ] 90168  #ifdef SQLITE_DEBUG
[ ] 90169    if( pOp->p4type==P4_TABLE
[ ] 90170     && HasRowid(pOp->p4.pTab)
[ ] 90171     && pOp->p5==0
[ ] 90172     && sqlite3BtreeCursorIsValidNN(pC->uc.pCursor)
[ ] 90173    ){
[ ] 90174      /* If p5 is zero, the seek operation that positioned the cursor prior to
[ ] 90175      ** OP_Delete will have also set the pC->movetoTarget field to the rowid of
[ ] 90176      ** the row that is being deleted */
[ ] 90177      i64 iKey = sqlite3BtreeIntegerKey(pC->uc.pCursor);
[ ] 90178      assert( CORRUPT_DB || pC->movetoTarget==iKey );
[ ] 90179    }
[ ] 90180  #endif
[ ] 90181
[ ] 90182    /* If the update-hook or pre-update-hook will be invoked, set zDb to
[ ] 90183    ** the name of the db to pass as to it. Also set local pTab to a copy
[ ] 90184    ** of p4.pTab. Finally, if p5 is true, indicating that this cursor was
[ ] 90185    ** last moved with OP_Next or OP_Prev, not Seek or NotFound, set
[ ] 90186    ** VdbeCursor.movetoTarget to the current rowid.  */
[ ] 90187    if( pOp->p4type==P4_TABLE && HAS_UPDATE_HOOK(db) ){
[ ] 90188      assert( pC->iDb>=0 );
[ ] 90189      assert( pOp->p4.pTab!=0 );
[ ] 90190      zDb = db->aDb[pC->iDb].zDbSName;
[ ] 90191      pTab = pOp->p4.pTab;
[ ] 90192      if( (pOp->p5 & OPFLAG_SAVEPOSITION)!=0 && pC->isTable ){
[ ] 90193        pC->movetoTarget = sqlite3BtreeIntegerKey(pC->uc.pCursor);
[ ] 90194      }
[ ] 90195    }else{
[ ] 90196      zDb = 0;   /* Not needed.  Silence a compiler warning. */
[ ] 90197      pTab = 0;  /* Not needed.  Silence a compiler warning. */
[ ] 90198    }
[ ] 90199
[ ] 90200  #ifdef SQLITE_ENABLE_PREUPDATE_HOOK
[ ] 90201    /* Invoke the pre-update-hook if required. */
[ ] 90202    if( db->xPreUpdateCallback && pOp->p4.pTab ){
[ ] 90203      assert( !(opflags & OPFLAG_ISUPDATE)
[ ] 90204           || HasRowid(pTab)==0
[ ] 90205           || (aMem[pOp->p3].flags & MEM_Int)
[ ] 90206      );
[ ] 90207      sqlite3VdbePreUpdateHook(p, pC,
[ ] 90208          (opflags & OPFLAG_ISUPDATE) ? SQLITE_UPDATE : SQLITE_DELETE,
[ ] 90209          zDb, pTab, pC->movetoTarget,
[ ] 90210          pOp->p3
[ ] 90211      );
[ ] 90212    }
[ ] 90213    if( opflags & OPFLAG_ISNOOP ) break;
[ ] 90214  #endif
[ ] 90215
[ ] 90216    /* Only flags that can be set are SAVEPOISTION and AUXDELETE */
[ ] 90217    assert( (pOp->p5 & ~(OPFLAG_SAVEPOSITION|OPFLAG_AUXDELETE))==0 );
[ ] 90218    assert( OPFLAG_SAVEPOSITION==BTREE_SAVEPOSITION );
[ ] 90219    assert( OPFLAG_AUXDELETE==BTREE_AUXDELETE );
[ ] 90220
[ ] 90221  #ifdef SQLITE_DEBUG
[ ] 90222    if( p->pFrame==0 ){
[ ] 90223      if( pC->isEphemeral==0
[ ] 90224          && (pOp->p5 & OPFLAG_AUXDELETE)==0
[ ] 90225          && (pC->wrFlag & OPFLAG_FORDELETE)==0
[ ] 90226        ){
[ ] 90227        nExtraDelete++;
[ ] 90228      }
[ ] 90229      if( pOp->p2 & OPFLAG_NCHANGE ){
[ ] 90230        nExtraDelete--;
[ ] 90231      }
[ ] 90232    }
[ ] 90233  #endif
[ ] 90234
[ ] 90235    rc = sqlite3BtreeDelete(pC->uc.pCursor, pOp->p5);
[ ] 90236    pC->cacheStatus = CACHE_STALE;
[ ] 90237    pC->seekResult = 0;
[ ] 90238    if( rc ) goto abort_due_to_error;
[ ] 90239
[ ] 90240    /* Invoke the update-hook if required. */
[ ] 90241    if( opflags & OPFLAG_NCHANGE ){
[ ] 90242      p->nChange++;
[ ] 90243      if( db->xUpdateCallback && HasRowid(pTab) ){
[ ] 90244        db->xUpdateCallback(db->pUpdateArg, SQLITE_DELETE, zDb, pTab->zName,
[ ] 90245            pC->movetoTarget);
[ ] 90246        assert( pC->iDb>=0 );
[ ] 90247      }
[ ] 90248    }
[ ] 90249
[ ] 90250    break;
[ ] 90251  }
[ ] 90252  /* Opcode: ResetCount * * * * *
[ ] 90253  **
[ ] 90254  ** The value of the change counter is copied to the database handle
[ ] 90255  ** change counter (returned by subsequent calls to sqlite3_changes()).
[ ] 90256  ** Then the VMs internal change counter resets to 0.
[ ] 90257  ** This is used by trigger programs.
[ ] 90258  */
[ ] 90259  case OP_ResetCount: {
[ ] 90260    sqlite3VdbeSetChanges(db, p->nChange);
[ ] 90261    p->nChange = 0;
[ ] 90262    break;
[ ] 90263  }
[ ] 90264
[ ] 90265  /* Opcode: SorterCompare P1 P2 P3 P4
[ ] 90266  ** Synopsis: if key(P1)!=trim(r[P3],P4) goto P2
[ ] 90267  **
[ ] 90268  ** P1 is a sorter cursor. This instruction compares a prefix of the
[ ] 90269  ** record blob in register P3 against a prefix of the entry that
[ ] 90270  ** the sorter cursor currently points to.  Only the first P4 fields
[ ] 90271  ** of r[P3] and the sorter record are compared.
[ ] 90272  **
[ ] 90273  ** If either P3 or the sorter contains a NULL in one of their significant
[ ] 90274  ** fields (not counting the P4 fields at the end which are ignored) then
[ ] 90275  ** the comparison is assumed to be equal.
[ ] 90276  **
[ ] 90277  ** Fall through to next instruction if the two records compare equal to
[ ] 90278  ** each other.  Jump to P2 if they are different.
[ ] 90279  */
[ ] 90280  case OP_SorterCompare: {
[ ] 90281    VdbeCursor *pC;
[ ] 90282    int res;
[ ] 90283    int nKeyCol;
[ ] 90284
[ ] 90285    pC = p->apCsr[pOp->p1];
[ ] 90286    assert( isSorter(pC) );
[ ] 90287    assert( pOp->p4type==P4_INT32 );
[ ] 90288    pIn3 = &aMem[pOp->p3];
[ ] 90289    nKeyCol = pOp->p4.i;
[ ] 90290    res = 0;
[ ] 90291    rc = sqlite3VdbeSorterCompare(pC, pIn3, nKeyCol, &res);
[ ] 90292    VdbeBranchTaken(res!=0,2);
[ ] 90293    if( rc ) goto abort_due_to_error;
[ ] 90294    if( res ) goto jump_to_p2;
[ ] 90295    break;
[ ] 90296  };
[ ] 90297
[ ] 90298  /* Opcode: SorterData P1 P2 P3 * *
[ ] 90299  ** Synopsis: r[P2]=data
[ ] 90300  **
[ ] 90301  ** Write into register P2 the current sorter data for sorter cursor P1.
[ ] 90302  ** Then clear the column header cache on cursor P3.
[ ] 90303  **
[ ] 90304  ** This opcode is normally use to move a record out of the sorter and into
[ ] 90305  ** a register that is the source for a pseudo-table cursor created using
[ ] 90306  ** OpenPseudo.  That pseudo-table cursor is the one that is identified by
[ ] 90307  ** parameter P3.  Clearing the P3 column cache as part of this opcode saves
[ ] 90308  ** us from having to issue a separate NullRow instruction to clear that cache.
[ ] 90309  */
[ ] 90310  case OP_SorterData: {
[ ] 90311    VdbeCursor *pC;
[ ] 90312
[ ] 90313    pOut = &aMem[pOp->p2];
[ ] 90314    pC = p->apCsr[pOp->p1];
[ ] 90315    assert( isSorter(pC) );
[ ] 90316    rc = sqlite3VdbeSorterRowkey(pC, pOut);
[ ] 90317    assert( rc!=SQLITE_OK || (pOut->flags & MEM_Blob) );
[ ] 90318    assert( pOp->p1>=0 && pOp->p1<p->nCursor );
[ ] 90319    if( rc ) goto abort_due_to_error;
[ ] 90320    p->apCsr[pOp->p3]->cacheStatus = CACHE_STALE;
[ ] 90321    break;
[ ] 90322  }
[ ] 90323
[ ] 90324  /* Opcode: RowData P1 P2 P3 * *
[ ] 90325  ** Synopsis: r[P2]=data
[ ] 90326  **
[ ] 90327  ** Write into register P2 the complete row content for the row at
[ ] 90328  ** which cursor P1 is currently pointing.
[ ] 90329  ** There is no interpretation of the data.
[ ] 90330  ** It is just copied onto the P2 register exactly as
[ ] 90331  ** it is found in the database file.
[ ] 90332  **
[ ] 90333  ** If cursor P1 is an index, then the content is the key of the row.
[ ] 90334  ** If cursor P2 is a table, then the content extracted is the data.
[ ] 90335  **
[ ] 90336  ** If the P1 cursor must be pointing to a valid row (not a NULL row)
[ ] 90337  ** of a real table, not a pseudo-table.
[ ] 90338  **
[ ] 90339  ** If P3!=0 then this opcode is allowed to make an ephemeral pointer
[ ] 90340  ** into the database page.  That means that the content of the output
[ ] 90341  ** register will be invalidated as soon as the cursor moves - including
[ ] 90342  ** moves caused by other cursors that "save" the current cursors
[ ] 90343  ** position in order that they can write to the same table.  If P3==0
[ ] 90344  ** then a copy of the data is made into memory.  P3!=0 is faster, but
[ ] 90345  ** P3==0 is safer.
[ ] 90346  **
[ ] 90347  ** If P3!=0 then the content of the P2 register is unsuitable for use
[ ] 90348  ** in OP_Result and any OP_Result will invalidate the P2 register content.
[ ] 90349  ** The P2 register content is invalidated by opcodes like OP_Function or
[ ] 90350  ** by any use of another cursor pointing to the same table.
[ ] 90351  */
[ ] 90352  case OP_RowData: {
[ ] 90353    VdbeCursor *pC;
[ ] 90354    BtCursor *pCrsr;
[ ] 90355    u32 n;
[ ] 90356
[ ] 90357    pOut = out2Prerelease(p, pOp);
[ ] 90358
[ ] 90359    assert( pOp->p1>=0 && pOp->p1<p->nCursor );
[ ] 90360    pC = p->apCsr[pOp->p1];
[ ] 90361    assert( pC!=0 );
[ ] 90362    assert( pC->eCurType==CURTYPE_BTREE );
[ ] 90363    assert( isSorter(pC)==0 );
[ ] 90364    assert( pC->nullRow==0 );
[ ] 90365    assert( pC->uc.pCursor!=0 );
[ ] 90366    pCrsr = pC->uc.pCursor;
[ ] 90367
[ ] 90368    /* The OP_RowData opcodes always follow OP_NotExists or
[ ] 90369    ** OP_SeekRowid or OP_Rewind/Op_Next with no intervening instructions
[ ] 90370    ** that might invalidate the cursor.
[ ] 90371    ** If this where not the case, on of the following assert()s
[ ] 90372    ** would fail.  Should this ever change (because of changes in the code
[ ] 90373    ** generator) then the fix would be to insert a call to
[ ] 90374    ** sqlite3VdbeCursorMoveto().
[ ] 90375    */
[ ] 90376    assert( pC->deferredMoveto==0 );
[ ] 90377    assert( sqlite3BtreeCursorIsValid(pCrsr) );
[ ] 90378  #if 0  /* Not required due to the previous to assert() statements */
[ ] 90379    rc = sqlite3VdbeCursorMoveto(pC);
[ ] 90380    if( rc!=SQLITE_OK ) goto abort_due_to_error;
[ ] 90381  #endif
[ ] 90382
[ ] 90383    n = sqlite3BtreePayloadSize(pCrsr);
[ ] 90384    if( n>(u32)db->aLimit[SQLITE_LIMIT_LENGTH] ){
[ ] 90385      goto too_big;
[ ] 90386    }
[ ] 90387    testcase( n==0 );
[ ] 90388    rc = sqlite3VdbeMemFromBtreeZeroOffset(pCrsr, n, pOut);
[ ] 90389    if( rc ) goto abort_due_to_error;
[ ] 90390    if( !pOp->p3 ) Deephemeralize(pOut);
[ ] 90391    UPDATE_MAX_BLOBSIZE(pOut);
[ ] 90392    REGISTER_TRACE(pOp->p2, pOut);
[ ] 90393    break;
[ ] 90394  }
[ ] 90395
[ ] 90396  /* Opcode: Rowid P1 P2 * * *
[ ] 90397  ** Synopsis: r[P2]=rowid
[ ] 90398  **
[ ] 90399  ** Store in register P2 an integer which is the key of the table entry that
[ ] 90400  ** P1 is currently point to.
[ ] 90401  **
[ ] 90402  ** P1 can be either an ordinary table or a virtual table.  There used to
[ ] 90403  ** be a separate OP_VRowid opcode for use with virtual tables, but this
[ ] 90404  ** one opcode now works for both table types.
[ ] 90405  */
[ ] 90406  case OP_Rowid: {                 /* out2 */
[ ] 90407    VdbeCursor *pC;
[ ] 90408    i64 v;
[ ] 90409    sqlite3_vtab *pVtab;
[ ] 90410    const sqlite3_module *pModule;
[ ] 90411
[ ] 90412    pOut = out2Prerelease(p, pOp);
[ ] 90413    assert( pOp->p1>=0 && pOp->p1<p->nCursor );
[ ] 90414    pC = p->apCsr[pOp->p1];
[ ] 90415    assert( pC!=0 );
[ ] 90416    assert( pC->eCurType!=CURTYPE_PSEUDO || pC->nullRow );
[ ] 90417    if( pC->nullRow ){
[ ] 90418      pOut->flags = MEM_Null;
[ ] 90419      break;
[ ] 90420    }else if( pC->deferredMoveto ){
[ ] 90421      v = pC->movetoTarget;
[ ] 90422  #ifndef SQLITE_OMIT_VIRTUALTABLE
[ ] 90423    }else if( pC->eCurType==CURTYPE_VTAB ){
[ ] 90424      assert( pC->uc.pVCur!=0 );
[ ] 90425      pVtab = pC->uc.pVCur->pVtab;
[ ] 90426      pModule = pVtab->pModule;
[ ] 90427      assert( pModule->xRowid );
[ ] 90428      rc = pModule->xRowid(pC->uc.pVCur, &v);
[ ] 90429      sqlite3VtabImportErrmsg(p, pVtab);
[ ] 90430      if( rc ) goto abort_due_to_error;
[ ] 90431  #endif /* SQLITE_OMIT_VIRTUALTABLE */
[ ] 90432    }else{
[ ] 90433      assert( pC->eCurType==CURTYPE_BTREE );
[ ] 90434      assert( pC->uc.pCursor!=0 );
[ ] 90435      rc = sqlite3VdbeCursorRestore(pC);
[ ] 90436      if( rc ) goto abort_due_to_error;
[ ] 90437      if( pC->nullRow ){
[ ] 90438        pOut->flags = MEM_Null;
[ ] 90439        break;
[ ] 90440      }
[ ] 90441      v = sqlite3BtreeIntegerKey(pC->uc.pCursor);
[ ] 90442    }
[ ] 90443    pOut->u.i = v;
[ ] 90444    break;
[ ] 90445  }
[ ] 90446
[ ] 90447  /* Opcode: NullRow P1 * * * *
[ ] 90448  **
[ ] 90449  ** Move the cursor P1 to a null row.  Any OP_Column operations
[ ] 90450  ** that occur while the cursor is on the null row will always
[ ] 90451  ** write a NULL.
[ ] 90452  */
[ ] 90453  case OP_NullRow: {
[ ] 90454    VdbeCursor *pC;
[ ] 90455
[ ] 90456    assert( pOp->p1>=0 && pOp->p1<p->nCursor );
[ ] 90457    pC = p->apCsr[pOp->p1];
[ ] 90458    assert( pC!=0 );
[ ] 90459    pC->nullRow = 1;
[ ] 90460    pC->cacheStatus = CACHE_STALE;
[ ] 90461    if( pC->eCurType==CURTYPE_BTREE ){
[ ] 90462      assert( pC->uc.pCursor!=0 );
[ ] 90463      sqlite3BtreeClearCursor(pC->uc.pCursor);
[ ] 90464    }
[ ] 90465  #ifdef SQLITE_DEBUG
[ ] 90466    if( pC->seekOp==0 ) pC->seekOp = OP_NullRow;
[ ] 90467  #endif
[ ] 90468    break;
[ ] 90469  }
[ ] 90470
[ ] 90471  /* Opcode: SeekEnd P1 * * * *
[ ] 90472  **
[ ] 90473  ** Position cursor P1 at the end of the btree for the purpose of
[ ] 90474  ** appending a new entry onto the btree.
[ ] 90475  **
[ ] 90476  ** It is assumed that the cursor is used only for appending and so
[ ] 90477  ** if the cursor is valid, then the cursor must already be pointing
[ ] 90478  ** at the end of the btree and so no changes are made to
[ ] 90479  ** the cursor.
[ ] 90480  */
[ ] 90481  /* Opcode: Last P1 P2 * * *
[ ] 90482  **
[ ] 90483  ** The next use of the Rowid or Column or Prev instruction for P1
[ ] 90484  ** will refer to the last entry in the database table or index.
[ ] 90485  ** If the table or index is empty and P2>0, then jump immediately to P2.
[ ] 90486  ** If P2 is 0 or if the table or index is not empty, fall through
[ ] 90487  ** to the following instruction.
[ ] 90488  **
[ ] 90489  ** This opcode leaves the cursor configured to move in reverse order,
[ ] 90490  ** from the end toward the beginning.  In other words, the cursor is
[ ] 90491  ** configured to use Prev, not Next.
[ ] 90492  */
[ ] 90493  case OP_SeekEnd:
[ ] 90494  case OP_Last: {        /* jump */
[ ] 90495    VdbeCursor *pC;
[ ] 90496    BtCursor *pCrsr;
[ ] 90497    int res;
[ ] 90498
[ ] 90499    assert( pOp->p1>=0 && pOp->p1<p->nCursor );
[ ] 90500    pC = p->apCsr[pOp->p1];
[ ] 90501    assert( pC!=0 );
[ ] 90502    assert( pC->eCurType==CURTYPE_BTREE );
[ ] 90503    pCrsr = pC->uc.pCursor;
[ ] 90504    res = 0;
[ ] 90505    assert( pCrsr!=0 );
[ ] 90506  #ifdef SQLITE_DEBUG
[ ] 90507    pC->seekOp = pOp->opcode;
[ ] 90508  #endif
[ ] 90509    if( pOp->opcode==OP_SeekEnd ){
[ ] 90510      assert( pOp->p2==0 );
[ ] 90511      pC->seekResult = -1;
[ ] 90512      if( sqlite3BtreeCursorIsValidNN(pCrsr) ){
[ ] 90513        break;
[ ] 90514      }
[ ] 90515    }
[ ] 90516    rc = sqlite3BtreeLast(pCrsr, &res);
[ ] 90517    pC->nullRow = (u8)res;
[ ] 90518    pC->deferredMoveto = 0;
[ ] 90519    pC->cacheStatus = CACHE_STALE;
[ ] 90520    if( rc ) goto abort_due_to_error;
[ ] 90521    if( pOp->p2>0 ){
[ ] 90522      VdbeBranchTaken(res!=0,2);
[ ] 90523      if( res ) goto jump_to_p2;
[ ] 90524    }
[ ] 90525    break;
[ ] 90526  }
[ ] 90527
[ ] 90528  /* Opcode: IfSmaller P1 P2 P3 * *
[ ] 90529  **
[ ] 90530  ** Estimate the number of rows in the table P1.  Jump to P2 if that
[ ] 90531  ** estimate is less than approximately 2**(0.1*P3).
[ ] 90532  */
[ ] 90533  case OP_IfSmaller: {        /* jump */
[ ] 90534    VdbeCursor *pC;
[ ] 90535    BtCursor *pCrsr;
[ ] 90536    int res;
[ ] 90537    i64 sz;
[ ] 90538
[ ] 90539    assert( pOp->p1>=0 && pOp->p1<p->nCursor );
[ ] 90540    pC = p->apCsr[pOp->p1];
[ ] 90541    assert( pC!=0 );
[ ] 90542    pCrsr = pC->uc.pCursor;
[ ] 90543    assert( pCrsr );
[ ] 90544    rc = sqlite3BtreeFirst(pCrsr, &res);
[ ] 90545    if( rc ) goto abort_due_to_error;
[ ] 90546    if( res==0 ){
[ ] 90547      sz = sqlite3BtreeRowCountEst(pCrsr);
[ ] 90548      if( ALWAYS(sz>=0) && sqlite3LogEst((u64)sz)<pOp->p3 ) res = 1;
[ ] 90549    }
[ ] 90550    VdbeBranchTaken(res!=0,2);
[ ] 90551    if( res ) goto jump_to_p2;
[ ] 90552    break;
[ ] 90553  }
[ ] 90554
[ ] 90555
[ ] 90556  /* Opcode: SorterSort P1 P2 * * *
[ ] 90557  **
[ ] 90558  ** After all records have been inserted into the Sorter object
[ ] 90559  ** identified by P1, invoke this opcode to actually do the sorting.
[ ] 90560  ** Jump to P2 if there are no records to be sorted.
[ ] 90561  **
[ ] 90562  ** This opcode is an alias for OP_Sort and OP_Rewind that is used
[ ] 90563  ** for Sorter objects.
[ ] 90564  */
[ ] 90565  /* Opcode: Sort P1 P2 * * *
[ ] 90566  **
[ ] 90567  ** This opcode does exactly the same thing as OP_Rewind except that
[ ] 90568  ** it increments an undocumented global variable used for testing.
[ ] 90569  **
[ ] 90570  ** Sorting is accomplished by writing records into a sorting index,
[ ] 90571  ** then rewinding that index and playing it back from beginning to
[ ] 90572  ** end.  We use the OP_Sort opcode instead of OP_Rewind to do the
[ ] 90573  ** rewinding so that the global variable will be incremented and
[ ] 90574  ** regression tests can determine whether or not the optimizer is
[ ] 90575  ** correctly optimizing out sorts.
[ ] 90576  */
[ ] 90577  case OP_SorterSort:    /* jump */
[ ] 90578  case OP_Sort: {        /* jump */
[ ] 90579  #ifdef SQLITE_TEST
[ ] 90580    sqlite3_sort_count++;
[ ] 90581    sqlite3_search_count--;
[ ] 90582  #endif
[ ] 90583    p->aCounter[SQLITE_STMTSTATUS_SORT]++;
[ ] 90584    /* Fall through into OP_Rewind */
[ ] 90585  }
[ ] 90586  /* Opcode: Rewind P1 P2 * * *
[ ] 90587  **
[ ] 90588  ** The next use of the Rowid or Column or Next instruction for P1
[ ] 90589  ** will refer to the first entry in the database table or index.
[ ] 90590  ** If the table or index is empty, jump immediately to P2.
[ ] 90591  ** If the table or index is not empty, fall through to the following
[ ] 90592  ** instruction.
[ ] 90593  **
[ ] 90594  ** This opcode leaves the cursor configured to move in forward order,
[ ] 90595  ** from the beginning toward the end.  In other words, the cursor is
[ ] 90596  ** configured to use Next, not Prev.
[ ] 90597  */
[ ] 90598  case OP_Rewind: {        /* jump */
[ ] 90599    VdbeCursor *pC;
[ ] 90600    BtCursor *pCrsr;
[ ] 90601    int res;
[ ] 90602
[ ] 90603    assert( pOp->p1>=0 && pOp->p1<p->nCursor );
[ ] 90604    assert( pOp->p5==0 );
[ ] 90605    pC = p->apCsr[pOp->p1];
[ ] 90606    assert( pC!=0 );
[ ] 90607    assert( isSorter(pC)==(pOp->opcode==OP_SorterSort) );
[ ] 90608    res = 1;
[ ] 90609  #ifdef SQLITE_DEBUG
[ ] 90610    pC->seekOp = OP_Rewind;
[ ] 90611  #endif
[ ] 90612    if( isSorter(pC) ){
[ ] 90613      rc = sqlite3VdbeSorterRewind(pC, &res);
[ ] 90614    }else{
[ ] 90615      assert( pC->eCurType==CURTYPE_BTREE );
[ ] 90616      pCrsr = pC->uc.pCursor;
[ ] 90617      assert( pCrsr );
[ ] 90618      rc = sqlite3BtreeFirst(pCrsr, &res);
[ ] 90619      pC->deferredMoveto = 0;
[ ] 90620      pC->cacheStatus = CACHE_STALE;
[ ] 90621    }
[ ] 90622    if( rc ) goto abort_due_to_error;
[ ] 90623    pC->nullRow = (u8)res;
[ ] 90624    assert( pOp->p2>0 && pOp->p2<p->nOp );
[ ] 90625    VdbeBranchTaken(res!=0,2);
[ ] 90626    if( res ) goto jump_to_p2;
[ ] 90627    break;
[ ] 90628  }
[ ] 90629
[ ] 90630  /* Opcode: Next P1 P2 P3 P4 P5
[ ] 90631  **
[ ] 90632  ** Advance cursor P1 so that it points to the next key/data pair in its
[ ] 90633  ** table or index.  If there are no more key/value pairs then fall through
[ ] 90634  ** to the following instruction.  But if the cursor advance was successful,
[ ] 90635  ** jump immediately to P2.
[ ] 90636  **
[ ] 90637  ** The Next opcode is only valid following an SeekGT, SeekGE, or
[ ] 90638  ** OP_Rewind opcode used to position the cursor.  Next is not allowed
[ ] 90639  ** to follow SeekLT, SeekLE, or OP_Last.
[ ] 90640  **
[ ] 90641  ** The P1 cursor must be for a real table, not a pseudo-table.  P1 must have
[ ] 90642  ** been opened prior to this opcode or the program will segfault.
[ ] 90643  **
[ ] 90644  ** The P3 value is a hint to the btree implementation. If P3==1, that
[ ] 90645  ** means P1 is an SQL index and that this instruction could have been
[ ] 90646  ** omitted if that index had been unique.  P3 is usually 0.  P3 is
[ ] 90647  ** always either 0 or 1.
[ ] 90648  **
[ ] 90649  ** P4 is always of type P4_ADVANCE. The function pointer points to
[ ] 90650  ** sqlite3BtreeNext().
[ ] 90651  **
[ ] 90652  ** If P5 is positive and the jump is taken, then event counter
[ ] 90653  ** number P5-1 in the prepared statement is incremented.
[ ] 90654  **
[ ] 90655  ** See also: Prev
[ ] 90656  */
[ ] 90657  /* Opcode: Prev P1 P2 P3 P4 P5
[ ] 90658  **
[ ] 90659  ** Back up cursor P1 so that it points to the previous key/data pair in its
[ ] 90660  ** table or index.  If there is no previous key/value pairs then fall through
[ ] 90661  ** to the following instruction.  But if the cursor backup was successful,
[ ] 90662  ** jump immediately to P2.
[ ] 90663  **
[ ] 90664  **
[ ] 90665  ** The Prev opcode is only valid following an SeekLT, SeekLE, or
[ ] 90666  ** OP_Last opcode used to position the cursor.  Prev is not allowed
[ ] 90667  ** to follow SeekGT, SeekGE, or OP_Rewind.
[ ] 90668  **
[ ] 90669  ** The P1 cursor must be for a real table, not a pseudo-table.  If P1 is
[ ] 90670  ** not open then the behavior is undefined.
[ ] 90671  **
[ ] 90672  ** The P3 value is a hint to the btree implementation. If P3==1, that
[ ] 90673  ** means P1 is an SQL index and that this instruction could have been
[ ] 90674  ** omitted if that index had been unique.  P3 is usually 0.  P3 is
[ ] 90675  ** always either 0 or 1.
[ ] 90676  **
[ ] 90677  ** P4 is always of type P4_ADVANCE. The function pointer points to
[ ] 90678  ** sqlite3BtreePrevious().
[ ] 90679  **
[ ] 90680  ** If P5 is positive and the jump is taken, then event counter
[ ] 90681  ** number P5-1 in the prepared statement is incremented.
[ ] 90682  */
[ ] 90683  /* Opcode: SorterNext P1 P2 * * P5
[ ] 90684  **
[ ] 90685  ** This opcode works just like OP_Next except that P1 must be a
[ ] 90686  ** sorter object for which the OP_SorterSort opcode has been
[ ] 90687  ** invoked.  This opcode advances the cursor to the next sorted
[ ] 90688  ** record, or jumps to P2 if there are no more sorted records.
[ ] 90689  */
[ ] 90690  case OP_SorterNext: {  /* jump */
[ ] 90691    VdbeCursor *pC;
[ ] 90692
[ ] 90693    pC = p->apCsr[pOp->p1];
[ ] 90694    assert( isSorter(pC) );
[ ] 90695    rc = sqlite3VdbeSorterNext(db, pC);
[ ] 90696    goto next_tail;
[ ] 90697  case OP_Prev:          /* jump */
[ ] 90698  case OP_Next:          /* jump */
[ ] 90699    assert( pOp->p1>=0 && pOp->p1<p->nCursor );
[ ] 90700    assert( pOp->p5<ArraySize(p->aCounter) );
[ ] 90701    pC = p->apCsr[pOp->p1];
[ ] 90702    assert( pC!=0 );
[ ] 90703    assert( pC->deferredMoveto==0 );
[ ] 90704    assert( pC->eCurType==CURTYPE_BTREE );
[ ] 90705    assert( pOp->opcode!=OP_Next || pOp->p4.xAdvance==sqlite3BtreeNext );
[ ] 90706    assert( pOp->opcode!=OP_Prev || pOp->p4.xAdvance==sqlite3BtreePrevious );
[ ] 90707
[ ] 90708    /* The Next opcode is only used after SeekGT, SeekGE, Rewind, and Found.
[ ] 90709    ** The Prev opcode is only used after SeekLT, SeekLE, and Last. */
[ ] 90710    assert( pOp->opcode!=OP_Next
[ ] 90711         || pC->seekOp==OP_SeekGT || pC->seekOp==OP_SeekGE
[ ] 90712         || pC->seekOp==OP_Rewind || pC->seekOp==OP_Found
[ ] 90713         || pC->seekOp==OP_NullRow|| pC->seekOp==OP_SeekRowid
[ ] 90714         || pC->seekOp==OP_IfNoHope);
[ ] 90715    assert( pOp->opcode!=OP_Prev
[ ] 90716         || pC->seekOp==OP_SeekLT || pC->seekOp==OP_SeekLE
[ ] 90717         || pC->seekOp==OP_Last   || pC->seekOp==OP_IfNoHope
[ ] 90718         || pC->seekOp==OP_NullRow);
[ ] 90719
[ ] 90720    rc = pOp->p4.xAdvance(pC->uc.pCursor, pOp->p3);
[ ] 90721  next_tail:
[ ] 90722    pC->cacheStatus = CACHE_STALE;
[ ] 90723    VdbeBranchTaken(rc==SQLITE_OK,2);
[ ] 90724    if( rc==SQLITE_OK ){
[ ] 90725      pC->nullRow = 0;
[ ] 90726      p->aCounter[pOp->p5]++;
[ ] 90727  #ifdef SQLITE_TEST
[ ] 90728      sqlite3_search_count++;
[ ] 90729  #endif
[ ] 90730      goto jump_to_p2_and_check_for_interrupt;
[ ] 90731    }
[ ] 90732    if( rc!=SQLITE_DONE ) goto abort_due_to_error;
[ ] 90733    rc = SQLITE_OK;
[ ] 90734    pC->nullRow = 1;
[ ] 90735    goto check_for_interrupt;
[ ] 90736  }
[ ] 90737
[ ] 90738  /* Opcode: IdxInsert P1 P2 P3 P4 P5
[ ] 90739  ** Synopsis: key=r[P2]
[ ] 90740  **
[ ] 90741  ** Register P2 holds an SQL index key made using the
[ ] 90742  ** MakeRecord instructions.  This opcode writes that key
[ ] 90743  ** into the index P1.  Data for the entry is nil.
[ ] 90744  **
[ ] 90745  ** If P4 is not zero, then it is the number of values in the unpacked
[ ] 90746  ** key of reg(P2).  In that case, P3 is the index of the first register
[ ] 90747  ** for the unpacked key.  The availability of the unpacked key can sometimes
[ ] 90748  ** be an optimization.
[ ] 90749  **
[ ] 90750  ** If P5 has the OPFLAG_APPEND bit set, that is a hint to the b-tree layer
[ ] 90751  ** that this insert is likely to be an append.
[ ] 90752  **
[ ] 90753  ** If P5 has the OPFLAG_NCHANGE bit set, then the change counter is
[ ] 90754  ** incremented by this instruction.  If the OPFLAG_NCHANGE bit is clear,
[ ] 90755  ** then the change counter is unchanged.
[ ] 90756  **
[ ] 90757  ** If the OPFLAG_USESEEKRESULT flag of P5 is set, the implementation might
[ ] 90758  ** run faster by avoiding an unnecessary seek on cursor P1.  However,
[ ] 90759  ** the OPFLAG_USESEEKRESULT flag must only be set if there have been no prior
[ ] 90760  ** seeks on the cursor or if the most recent seek used a key equivalent
[ ] 90761  ** to P2.
[ ] 90762  **
[ ] 90763  ** This instruction only works for indices.  The equivalent instruction
[ ] 90764  ** for tables is OP_Insert.
[ ] 90765  */
[ ] 90766  case OP_IdxInsert: {        /* in2 */
[ ] 90767    VdbeCursor *pC;
[ ] 90768    BtreePayload x;
[ ] 90769
[ ] 90770    assert( pOp->p1>=0 && pOp->p1<p->nCursor );
[ ] 90771    pC = p->apCsr[pOp->p1];
[ ] 90772    sqlite3VdbeIncrWriteCounter(p, pC);
[ ] 90773    assert( pC!=0 );
[ ] 90774    assert( !isSorter(pC) );
[ ] 90775    pIn2 = &aMem[pOp->p2];
[ ] 90776    assert( pIn2->flags & MEM_Blob );
[ ] 90777    if( pOp->p5 & OPFLAG_NCHANGE ) p->nChange++;
[ ] 90778    assert( pC->eCurType==CURTYPE_BTREE );
[ ] 90779    assert( pC->isTable==0 );
[ ] 90780    rc = ExpandBlob(pIn2);
[ ] 90781    if( rc ) goto abort_due_to_error;
[ ] 90782    x.nKey = pIn2->n;
[ ] 90783    x.pKey = pIn2->z;
[ ] 90784    x.aMem = aMem + pOp->p3;
[ ] 90785    x.nMem = (u16)pOp->p4.i;
[ ] 90786    rc = sqlite3BtreeInsert(pC->uc.pCursor, &x,
[ ] 90787         (pOp->p5 & (OPFLAG_APPEND|OPFLAG_SAVEPOSITION)),
[ ] 90788        ((pOp->p5 & OPFLAG_USESEEKRESULT) ? pC->seekResult : 0)
[ ] 90789        );
[ ] 90790    assert( pC->deferredMoveto==0 );
[ ] 90791    pC->cacheStatus = CACHE_STALE;
[ ] 90792    if( rc) goto abort_due_to_error;
[ ] 90793    break;
[ ] 90794  }
[ ] 90795
[ ] 90796  /* Opcode: SorterInsert P1 P2 * * *
[ ] 90797  ** Synopsis: key=r[P2]
[ ] 90798  **
[ ] 90799  ** Register P2 holds an SQL index key made using the
[ ] 90800  ** MakeRecord instructions.  This opcode writes that key
[ ] 90801  ** into the sorter P1.  Data for the entry is nil.
[ ] 90802  */
[ ] 90803  case OP_SorterInsert: {     /* in2 */
[ ] 90804    VdbeCursor *pC;
[ ] 90805
[ ] 90806    assert( pOp->p1>=0 && pOp->p1<p->nCursor );
[ ] 90807    pC = p->apCsr[pOp->p1];
[ ] 90808    sqlite3VdbeIncrWriteCounter(p, pC);
[ ] 90809    assert( pC!=0 );
[ ] 90810    assert( isSorter(pC) );
[ ] 90811    pIn2 = &aMem[pOp->p2];
[ ] 90812    assert( pIn2->flags & MEM_Blob );
[ ] 90813    assert( pC->isTable==0 );
[ ] 90814    rc = ExpandBlob(pIn2);
[ ] 90815    if( rc ) goto abort_due_to_error;
[ ] 90816    rc = sqlite3VdbeSorterWrite(pC, pIn2);
[ ] 90817    if( rc) goto abort_due_to_error;
[ ] 90818    break;
[ ] 90819  }
[ ] 90820
[ ] 90821  /* Opcode: IdxDelete P1 P2 P3 * P5
[ ] 90822  ** Synopsis: key=r[P2@P3]
[ ] 90823  **
[ ] 90824  ** The content of P3 registers starting at register P2 form
[ ] 90825  ** an unpacked index key. This opcode removes that entry from the
[ ] 90826  ** index opened by cursor P1.
[ ] 90827  **
[ ] 90828  ** If P5 is not zero, then raise an SQLITE_CORRUPT_INDEX error
[ ] 90829  ** if no matching index entry is found.  This happens when running
[ ] 90830  ** an UPDATE or DELETE statement and the index entry to be updated
[ ] 90831  ** or deleted is not found.  For some uses of IdxDelete
[ ] 90832  ** (example:  the EXCEPT operator) it does not matter that no matching
[ ] 90833  ** entry is found.  For those cases, P5 is zero.
[ ] 90834  */
[ ] 90835  case OP_IdxDelete: {
[ ] 90836    VdbeCursor *pC;
[ ] 90837    BtCursor *pCrsr;
[ ] 90838    int res;
[ ] 90839    UnpackedRecord r;
[ ] 90840
[ ] 90841    assert( pOp->p3>0 );
[ ] 90842    assert( pOp->p2>0 && pOp->p2+pOp->p3<=(p->nMem+1 - p->nCursor)+1 );
[ ] 90843    assert( pOp->p1>=0 && pOp->p1<p->nCursor );
[ ] 90844    pC = p->apCsr[pOp->p1];
[ ] 90845    assert( pC!=0 );
[ ] 90846    assert( pC->eCurType==CURTYPE_BTREE );
[ ] 90847    sqlite3VdbeIncrWriteCounter(p, pC);
[ ] 90848    pCrsr = pC->uc.pCursor;
[ ] 90849    assert( pCrsr!=0 );
[ ] 90850    r.pKeyInfo = pC->pKeyInfo;
[ ] 90851    r.nField = (u16)pOp->p3;
[ ] 90852    r.default_rc = 0;
[ ] 90853    r.aMem = &aMem[pOp->p2];
[ ] 90854    rc = sqlite3BtreeMovetoUnpacked(pCrsr, &r, 0, 0, &res);
[ ] 90855    if( rc ) goto abort_due_to_error;
[ ] 90856    if( res==0 ){
[ ] 90857      rc = sqlite3BtreeDelete(pCrsr, BTREE_AUXDELETE);
[ ] 90858      if( rc ) goto abort_due_to_error;
[ ] 90859    }else if( pOp->p5 ){
[ ] 90860      rc = SQLITE_CORRUPT_INDEX;
[ ] 90861      goto abort_due_to_error;
[ ] 90862    }
[ ] 90863    assert( pC->deferredMoveto==0 );
[ ] 90864    pC->cacheStatus = CACHE_STALE;
[ ] 90865    pC->seekResult = 0;
[ ] 90866    break;
[ ] 90867  }
[ ] 90868
[ ] 90869  /* Opcode: DeferredSeek P1 * P3 P4 *
[ ] 90870  ** Synopsis: Move P3 to P1.rowid if needed
[ ] 90871  **
[ ] 90872  ** P1 is an open index cursor and P3 is a cursor on the corresponding
[ ] 90873  ** table.  This opcode does a deferred seek of the P3 table cursor
[ ] 90874  ** to the row that corresponds to the current row of P1.
[ ] 90875  **
[ ] 90876  ** This is a deferred seek.  Nothing actually happens until
[ ] 90877  ** the cursor is used to read a record.  That way, if no reads
[ ] 90878  ** occur, no unnecessary I/O happens.
[ ] 90879  **
[ ] 90880  ** P4 may be an array of integers (type P4_INTARRAY) containing
[ ] 90881  ** one entry for each column in the P3 table.  If array entry a(i)
[ ] 90882  ** is non-zero, then reading column a(i)-1 from cursor P3 is
[ ] 90883  ** equivalent to performing the deferred seek and then reading column i
[ ] 90884  ** from P1.  This information is stored in P3 and used to redirect
[ ] 90885  ** reads against P3 over to P1, thus possibly avoiding the need to
[ ] 90886  ** seek and read cursor P3.
[ ] 90887  */
[ ] 90888  /* Opcode: IdxRowid P1 P2 * * *
[ ] 90889  ** Synopsis: r[P2]=rowid
[ ] 90890  **
[ ] 90891  ** Write into register P2 an integer which is the last entry in the record at
[ ] 90892  ** the end of the index key pointed to by cursor P1.  This integer should be
[ ] 90893  ** the rowid of the table entry to which this index entry points.
[ ] 90894  **
[ ] 90895  ** See also: Rowid, MakeRecord.
[ ] 90896  */
[ ] 90897  case OP_DeferredSeek:
[ ] 90898  case OP_IdxRowid: {           /* out2 */
[ ] 90899    VdbeCursor *pC;             /* The P1 index cursor */
[ ] 90900    VdbeCursor *pTabCur;        /* The P2 table cursor (OP_DeferredSeek only) */
[ ] 90901    i64 rowid;                  /* Rowid that P1 current points to */
[ ] 90902
[ ] 90903    assert( pOp->p1>=0 && pOp->p1<p->nCursor );
[ ] 90904    pC = p->apCsr[pOp->p1];
[ ] 90905    assert( pC!=0 );
[ ] 90906    assert( pC->eCurType==CURTYPE_BTREE );
[ ] 90907    assert( pC->uc.pCursor!=0 );
[ ] 90908    assert( pC->isTable==0 );
[ ] 90909    assert( pC->deferredMoveto==0 );
[ ] 90910    assert( !pC->nullRow || pOp->opcode==OP_IdxRowid );
[ ] 90911
[ ] 90912    /* The IdxRowid and Seek opcodes are combined because of the commonality
[ ] 90913    ** of sqlite3VdbeCursorRestore() and sqlite3VdbeIdxRowid(). */
[ ] 90914    rc = sqlite3VdbeCursorRestore(pC);
[ ] 90915
[ ] 90916    /* sqlite3VbeCursorRestore() can only fail if the record has been deleted
[ ] 90917    ** out from under the cursor.  That will never happens for an IdxRowid
[ ] 90918    ** or Seek opcode */
[ ] 90919    if( NEVER(rc!=SQLITE_OK) ) goto abort_due_to_error;
[ ] 90920
[ ] 90921    if( !pC->nullRow ){
[ ] 90922      rowid = 0;  /* Not needed.  Only used to silence a warning. */
[ ] 90923      rc = sqlite3VdbeIdxRowid(db, pC->uc.pCursor, &rowid);
[ ] 90924      if( rc!=SQLITE_OK ){
[ ] 90925        goto abort_due_to_error;
[ ] 90926      }
[ ] 90927      if( pOp->opcode==OP_DeferredSeek ){
[ ] 90928        assert( pOp->p3>=0 && pOp->p3<p->nCursor );
[ ] 90929        pTabCur = p->apCsr[pOp->p3];
[ ] 90930        assert( pTabCur!=0 );
[ ] 90931        assert( pTabCur->eCurType==CURTYPE_BTREE );
[ ] 90932        assert( pTabCur->uc.pCursor!=0 );
[ ] 90933        assert( pTabCur->isTable );
[ ] 90934        pTabCur->nullRow = 0;
[ ] 90935        pTabCur->movetoTarget = rowid;
[ ] 90936        pTabCur->deferredMoveto = 1;
[ ] 90937        assert( pOp->p4type==P4_INTARRAY || pOp->p4.ai==0 );
[ ] 90938        pTabCur->aAltMap = pOp->p4.ai;
[ ] 90939        pTabCur->pAltCursor = pC;
[ ] 90940      }else{
[ ] 90941        pOut = out2Prerelease(p, pOp);
[ ] 90942        pOut->u.i = rowid;
[ ] 90943      }
[ ] 90944    }else{
[ ] 90945      assert( pOp->opcode==OP_IdxRowid );
[ ] 90946      sqlite3VdbeMemSetNull(&aMem[pOp->p2]);
[ ] 90947    }
[ ] 90948    break;
[ ] 90949  }
[ ] 90950
[ ] 90951  /* Opcode: FinishSeek P1 * * * *
[ ] 90952  **
[ ] 90953  ** If cursor P1 was previously moved via OP_DeferredSeek, complete that
[ ] 90954  ** seek operation now, without further delay.  If the cursor seek has
[ ] 90955  ** already occurred, this instruction is a no-op.
[ ] 90956  */
[ ] 90957  case OP_FinishSeek: {
[ ] 90958    VdbeCursor *pC;             /* The P1 index cursor */
[ ] 90959
[ ] 90960    assert( pOp->p1>=0 && pOp->p1<p->nCursor );
[ ] 90961    pC = p->apCsr[pOp->p1];
[ ] 90962    if( pC->deferredMoveto ){
[ ] 90963      rc = sqlite3VdbeFinishMoveto(pC);
[ ] 90964      if( rc ) goto abort_due_to_error;
[ ] 90965    }
[ ] 90966    break;
[ ] 90967  }
[ ] 90968
[ ] 90969  /* Opcode: IdxGE P1 P2 P3 P4 P5
[ ] 90970  ** Synopsis: key=r[P3@P4]
[ ] 90971  **
[ ] 90972  ** The P4 register values beginning with P3 form an unpacked index
[ ] 90973  ** key that omits the PRIMARY KEY.  Compare this key value against the index
[ ] 90974  ** that P1 is currently pointing to, ignoring the PRIMARY KEY or ROWID
[ ] 90975  ** fields at the end.
[ ] 90976  **
[ ] 90977  ** If the P1 index entry is greater than or equal to the key value
[ ] 90978  ** then jump to P2.  Otherwise fall through to the next instruction.
[ ] 90979  */
[ ] 90980  /* Opcode: IdxGT P1 P2 P3 P4 P5
[ ] 90981  ** Synopsis: key=r[P3@P4]
[ ] 90982  **
[ ] 90983  ** The P4 register values beginning with P3 form an unpacked index
[ ] 90984  ** key that omits the PRIMARY KEY.  Compare this key value against the index
[ ] 90985  ** that P1 is currently pointing to, ignoring the PRIMARY KEY or ROWID
[ ] 90986  ** fields at the end.
[ ] 90987  **
[ ] 90988  ** If the P1 index entry is greater than the key value
[ ] 90989  ** then jump to P2.  Otherwise fall through to the next instruction.
[ ] 90990  */
[ ] 90991  /* Opcode: IdxLT P1 P2 P3 P4 P5
[ ] 90992  ** Synopsis: key=r[P3@P4]
[ ] 90993  **
[ ] 90994  ** The P4 register values beginning with P3 form an unpacked index
[ ] 90995  ** key that omits the PRIMARY KEY or ROWID.  Compare this key value against
[ ] 90996  ** the index that P1 is currently pointing to, ignoring the PRIMARY KEY or
[ ] 90997  ** ROWID on the P1 index.
[ ] 90998  **
[ ] 90999  ** If the P1 index entry is less than the key value then jump to P2.
[ ] 91000  ** Otherwise fall through to the next instruction.
[ ] 91001  */
[ ] 91002  /* Opcode: IdxLE P1 P2 P3 P4 P5
[ ] 91003  ** Synopsis: key=r[P3@P4]
[ ] 91004  **
[ ] 91005  ** The P4 register values beginning with P3 form an unpacked index
[ ] 91006  ** key that omits the PRIMARY KEY or ROWID.  Compare this key value against
[ ] 91007  ** the index that P1 is currently pointing to, ignoring the PRIMARY KEY or
[ ] 91008  ** ROWID on the P1 index.
[ ] 91009  **
[ ] 91010  ** If the P1 index entry is less than or equal to the key value then jump
[ ] 91011  ** to P2. Otherwise fall through to the next instruction.
[ ] 91012  */
[ ] 91013  case OP_IdxLE:          /* jump */
[ ] 91014  case OP_IdxGT:          /* jump */
[ ] 91015  case OP_IdxLT:          /* jump */
[ ] 91016  case OP_IdxGE:  {       /* jump */
[ ] 91017    VdbeCursor *pC;
[ ] 91018    int res;
[ ] 91019    UnpackedRecord r;
[ ] 91020
[ ] 91021    assert( pOp->p1>=0 && pOp->p1<p->nCursor );
[ ] 91022    pC = p->apCsr[pOp->p1];
[ ] 91023    assert( pC!=0 );
[ ] 91024    assert( pC->isOrdered );
[ ] 91025    assert( pC->eCurType==CURTYPE_BTREE );
[ ] 91026    assert( pC->uc.pCursor!=0);
[ ] 91027    assert( pC->deferredMoveto==0 );
[ ] 91028    assert( pOp->p5==0 || pOp->p5==1 );
[ ] 91029    assert( pOp->p4type==P4_INT32 );
[ ] 91030    r.pKeyInfo = pC->pKeyInfo;
[ ] 91031    r.nField = (u16)pOp->p4.i;
[ ] 91032    if( pOp->opcode<OP_IdxLT ){
[ ] 91033      assert( pOp->opcode==OP_IdxLE || pOp->opcode==OP_IdxGT );
[ ] 91034      r.default_rc = -1;
[ ] 91035    }else{
[ ] 91036      assert( pOp->opcode==OP_IdxGE || pOp->opcode==OP_IdxLT );
[ ] 91037      r.default_rc = 0;
[ ] 91038    }
[ ] 91039    r.aMem = &aMem[pOp->p3];
[ ] 91040  #ifdef SQLITE_DEBUG
[ ] 91041    {
[ ] 91042      int i;
[ ] 91043      for(i=0; i<r.nField; i++){
[ ] 91044        assert( memIsValid(&r.aMem[i]) );
[ ] 91045        REGISTER_TRACE(pOp->p3+i, &aMem[pOp->p3+i]);
[ ] 91046      }
[ ] 91047    }
[ ] 91048  #endif
[ ] 91049    res = 0;  /* Not needed.  Only used to silence a warning. */
[ ] 91050    rc = sqlite3VdbeIdxKeyCompare(db, pC, &r, &res);
[ ] 91051    assert( (OP_IdxLE&1)==(OP_IdxLT&1) && (OP_IdxGE&1)==(OP_IdxGT&1) );
[ ] 91052    if( (pOp->opcode&1)==(OP_IdxLT&1) ){
[ ] 91053      assert( pOp->opcode==OP_IdxLE || pOp->opcode==OP_IdxLT );
[ ] 91054      res = -res;
[ ] 91055    }else{
[ ] 91056      assert( pOp->opcode==OP_IdxGE || pOp->opcode==OP_IdxGT );
[ ] 91057      res++;
[ ] 91058    }
[ ] 91059    VdbeBranchTaken(res>0,2);
[ ] 91060    if( rc ) goto abort_due_to_error;
[ ] 91061    if( res>0 ) goto jump_to_p2;
[ ] 91062    break;
[ ] 91063  }
[ ] 91064
[ ] 91065  /* Opcode: Destroy P1 P2 P3 * *
[ ] 91066  **
[ ] 91067  ** Delete an entire database table or index whose root page in the database
[ ] 91068  ** file is given by P1.
[ ] 91069  **
[ ] 91070  ** The table being destroyed is in the main database file if P3==0.  If
[ ] 91071  ** P3==1 then the table to be clear is in the auxiliary database file
[ ] 91072  ** that is used to store tables create using CREATE TEMPORARY TABLE.
[ ] 91073  **
[ ] 91074  ** If AUTOVACUUM is enabled then it is possible that another root page
[ ] 91075  ** might be moved into the newly deleted root page in order to keep all
[ ] 91076  ** root pages contiguous at the beginning of the database.  The former
[ ] 91077  ** value of the root page that moved - its value before the move occurred -
[ ] 91078  ** is stored in register P2. If no page movement was required (because the
[ ] 91079  ** table being dropped was already the last one in the database) then a
[ ] 91080  ** zero is stored in register P2.  If AUTOVACUUM is disabled then a zero
[ ] 91081  ** is stored in register P2.
[ ] 91082  **
[ ] 91083  ** This opcode throws an error if there are any active reader VMs when
[ ] 91084  ** it is invoked. This is done to avoid the difficulty associated with
[ ] 91085  ** updating existing cursors when a root page is moved in an AUTOVACUUM
[ ] 91086  ** database. This error is thrown even if the database is not an AUTOVACUUM
[ ] 91087  ** db in order to avoid introducing an incompatibility between autovacuum
[ ] 91088  ** and non-autovacuum modes.
[ ] 91089  **
[ ] 91090  ** See also: Clear
[ ] 91091  */
[ ] 91092  case OP_Destroy: {     /* out2 */
[ ] 91093    int iMoved;
[ ] 91094    int iDb;
[ ] 91095
[ ] 91096    sqlite3VdbeIncrWriteCounter(p, 0);
[ ] 91097    assert( p->readOnly==0 );
[ ] 91098    assert( pOp->p1>1 );
[ ] 91099    pOut = out2Prerelease(p, pOp);
[ ] 91100    pOut->flags = MEM_Null;
[ ] 91101    if( db->nVdbeRead > db->nVDestroy+1 ){
[ ] 91102      rc = SQLITE_LOCKED;
[ ] 91103      p->errorAction = OE_Abort;
[ ] 91104      goto abort_due_to_error;
[ ] 91105    }else{
[ ] 91106      iDb = pOp->p3;
[ ] 91107      assert( DbMaskTest(p->btreeMask, iDb) );
[ ] 91108      iMoved = 0;  /* Not needed.  Only to silence a warning. */
[ ] 91109      rc = sqlite3BtreeDropTable(db->aDb[iDb].pBt, pOp->p1, &iMoved);
[ ] 91110      pOut->flags = MEM_Int;
[ ] 91111      pOut->u.i = iMoved;
[ ] 91112      if( rc ) goto abort_due_to_error;
[ ] 91113  #ifndef SQLITE_OMIT_AUTOVACUUM
[ ] 91114      if( iMoved!=0 ){
[ ] 91115        sqlite3RootPageMoved(db, iDb, iMoved, pOp->p1);
[ ] 91116        /* All OP_Destroy operations occur on the same btree */
[ ] 91117        assert( resetSchemaOnFault==0 || resetSchemaOnFault==iDb+1 );
[ ] 91118        resetSchemaOnFault = iDb+1;
[ ] 91119      }
[ ] 91120  #endif
[ ] 91121    }
[ ] 91122    break;
[ ] 91123  }
[ ] 91124
[ ] 91125  /* Opcode: Clear P1 P2 P3
[ ] 91126  **
[ ] 91127  ** Delete all contents of the database table or index whose root page
[ ] 91128  ** in the database file is given by P1.  But, unlike Destroy, do not
[ ] 91129  ** remove the table or index from the database file.
[ ] 91130  **
[ ] 91131  ** The table being clear is in the main database file if P2==0.  If
[ ] 91132  ** P2==1 then the table to be clear is in the auxiliary database file
[ ] 91133  ** that is used to store tables create using CREATE TEMPORARY TABLE.
[ ] 91134  **
[ ] 91135  ** If the P3 value is non-zero, then the table referred to must be an
[ ] 91136  ** intkey table (an SQL table, not an index). In this case the row change
[ ] 91137  ** count is incremented by the number of rows in the table being cleared.
[ ] 91138  ** If P3 is greater than zero, then the value stored in register P3 is
[ ] 91139  ** also incremented by the number of rows in the table being cleared.
[ ] 91140  **
[ ] 91141  ** See also: Destroy
[ ] 91142  */
[ ] 91143  case OP_Clear: {
[ ] 91144    int nChange;
[ ] 91145
[ ] 91146    sqlite3VdbeIncrWriteCounter(p, 0);
[ ] 91147    nChange = 0;
[ ] 91148    assert( p->readOnly==0 );
[ ] 91149    assert( DbMaskTest(p->btreeMask, pOp->p2) );
[ ] 91150    rc = sqlite3BtreeClearTable(
[ ] 91151        db->aDb[pOp->p2].pBt, pOp->p1, (pOp->p3 ? &nChange : 0)
[ ] 91152    );
[ ] 91153    if( pOp->p3 ){
[ ] 91154      p->nChange += nChange;
[ ] 91155      if( pOp->p3>0 ){
[ ] 91156        assert( memIsValid(&aMem[pOp->p3]) );
[ ] 91157        memAboutToChange(p, &aMem[pOp->p3]);
[ ] 91158        aMem[pOp->p3].u.i += nChange;
[ ] 91159      }
[ ] 91160    }
[ ] 91161    if( rc ) goto abort_due_to_error;
[ ] 91162    break;
[ ] 91163  }
[ ] 91164
[ ] 91165  /* Opcode: ResetSorter P1 * * * *
[ ] 91166  **
[ ] 91167  ** Delete all contents from the ephemeral table or sorter
[ ] 91168  ** that is open on cursor P1.
[ ] 91169  **
[ ] 91170  ** This opcode only works for cursors used for sorting and
[ ] 91171  ** opened with OP_OpenEphemeral or OP_SorterOpen.
[ ] 91172  */
[ ] 91173  case OP_ResetSorter: {
[ ] 91174    VdbeCursor *pC;
[ ] 91175
[ ] 91176    assert( pOp->p1>=0 && pOp->p1<p->nCursor );
[ ] 91177    pC = p->apCsr[pOp->p1];
[ ] 91178    assert( pC!=0 );
[ ] 91179    if( isSorter(pC) ){
[ ] 91180      sqlite3VdbeSorterReset(db, pC->uc.pSorter);
[ ] 91181    }else{
[ ] 91182      assert( pC->eCurType==CURTYPE_BTREE );
[ ] 91183      assert( pC->isEphemeral );
[ ] 91184      rc = sqlite3BtreeClearTableOfCursor(pC->uc.pCursor);
[ ] 91185      if( rc ) goto abort_due_to_error;
[ ] 91186    }
[ ] 91187    break;
[ ] 91188  }
[ ] 91189
[ ] 91190  /* Opcode: CreateBtree P1 P2 P3 * *
[ ] 91191  ** Synopsis: r[P2]=root iDb=P1 flags=P3
[ ] 91192  **
[ ] 91193  ** Allocate a new b-tree in the main database file if P1==0 or in the
[ ] 91194  ** TEMP database file if P1==1 or in an attached database if
[ ] 91195  ** P1>1.  The P3 argument must be 1 (BTREE_INTKEY) for a rowid table
[ ] 91196  ** it must be 2 (BTREE_BLOBKEY) for an index or WITHOUT ROWID table.
[ ] 91197  ** The root page number of the new b-tree is stored in register P2.
[ ] 91198  */
[ ] 91199  case OP_CreateBtree: {          /* out2 */
[ ] 91200    int pgno;
[ ] 91201    Db *pDb;
[ ] 91202
[ ] 91203    sqlite3VdbeIncrWriteCounter(p, 0);
[ ] 91204    pOut = out2Prerelease(p, pOp);
[ ] 91205    pgno = 0;
[ ] 91206    assert( pOp->p3==BTREE_INTKEY || pOp->p3==BTREE_BLOBKEY );
[ ] 91207    assert( pOp->p1>=0 && pOp->p1<db->nDb );
[ ] 91208    assert( DbMaskTest(p->btreeMask, pOp->p1) );
[ ] 91209    assert( p->readOnly==0 );
[ ] 91210    pDb = &db->aDb[pOp->p1];
[ ] 91211    assert( pDb->pBt!=0 );
[ ] 91212    rc = sqlite3BtreeCreateTable(pDb->pBt, &pgno, pOp->p3);
[ ] 91213    if( rc ) goto abort_due_to_error;
[ ] 91214    pOut->u.i = pgno;
[ ] 91215    break;
[ ] 91216  }
[ ] 91217
[ ] 91218  /* Opcode: SqlExec * * * P4 *
[ ] 91219  **
[ ] 91220  ** Run the SQL statement or statements specified in the P4 string.
[ ] 91221  */
[ ] 91222  case OP_SqlExec: {
[ ] 91223    sqlite3VdbeIncrWriteCounter(p, 0);
[ ] 91224    db->nSqlExec++;
[ ] 91225    rc = sqlite3_exec(db, pOp->p4.z, 0, 0, 0);
[ ] 91226    db->nSqlExec--;
[ ] 91227    if( rc ) goto abort_due_to_error;
[ ] 91228    break;
[ ] 91229  }
[ ] 91230
[ ] 91231  /* Opcode: ParseSchema P1 * * P4 *
[ ] 91232  **
[ ] 91233  ** Read and parse all entries from the schema table of database P1
[ ] 91234  ** that match the WHERE clause P4.  If P4 is a NULL pointer, then the
[ ] 91235  ** entire schema for P1 is reparsed.
[ ] 91236  **
[ ] 91237  ** This opcode invokes the parser to create a new virtual machine,
[ ] 91238  ** then runs the new virtual machine.  It is thus a re-entrant opcode.
[ ] 91239  */
[ ] 91240  case OP_ParseSchema: {
[ ] 91241    int iDb;
[ ] 91242    const char *zSchema;
[ ] 91243    char *zSql;
[ ] 91244    InitData initData;
[ ] 91245
[ ] 91246    /* Any prepared statement that invokes this opcode will hold mutexes
[ ] 91247    ** on every btree.  This is a prerequisite for invoking
[ ] 91248    ** sqlite3InitCallback().
[ ] 91249    */
[ ] 91250  #ifdef SQLITE_DEBUG
[ ] 91251    for(iDb=0; iDb<db->nDb; iDb++){
[ ] 91252      assert( iDb==1 || sqlite3BtreeHoldsMutex(db->aDb[iDb].pBt) );
[ ] 91253    }
[ ] 91254  #endif
[ ] 91255
[ ] 91256    iDb = pOp->p1;
[ ] 91257    assert( iDb>=0 && iDb<db->nDb );
[ ] 91258    assert( DbHasProperty(db, iDb, DB_SchemaLoaded) );
[ ] 91259
[ ] 91260  #ifndef SQLITE_OMIT_ALTERTABLE
[ ] 91261    if( pOp->p4.z==0 ){
[ ] 91262      sqlite3SchemaClear(db->aDb[iDb].pSchema);
[ ] 91263      db->mDbFlags &= ~DBFLAG_SchemaKnownOk;
[ ] 91264      rc = sqlite3InitOne(db, iDb, &p->zErrMsg, INITFLAG_AlterTable);
[ ] 91265      db->mDbFlags |= DBFLAG_SchemaChange;
[ ] 91266      p->expired = 0;
[ ] 91267    }else
[ ] 91268  #endif
[ ] 91269    {
[ ] 91270      zSchema = DFLT_SCHEMA_TABLE;
[ ] 91271      initData.db = db;
[ ] 91272      initData.iDb = iDb;
[ ] 91273      initData.pzErrMsg = &p->zErrMsg;
[ ] 91274      initData.mInitFlags = 0;
[ ] 91275      zSql = sqlite3MPrintf(db,
